
-----title

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年</a>　居乡。以艺业试乡校选，迥出流辈。丁父忧，勤奋治学，律身甚严。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1103&endYear=1103')">1103年</a>　居乡，在乡校读书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1104&endYear=1104')">1104年</a>　在乡校，被荐名乡书，作谢启。试太学生选，有声名。作品：《谢荐举启》<br /></div><div class='label1' id='1cecad995ece4137ba27a7f5c4aa09bc_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1119&endYear=1119')">1119年</a>　归德清，丁内艰。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1121')">1120-1121年</a>　在德清，居丧。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='aeefacf49a9b47a6aed7a7d58feb723f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("aeefacf49a9b47a6aed7a7d58feb723f");'><span id='aeefacf49a9b47a6aed7a7d58feb723f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年</a>，44岁</div><div id='aeefacf49a9b47a6aed7a7d58feb723f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年</a>　年底，在白彪与张元干游，有诗。作品：《次韵张仲宗感事》<div id='poem_538701' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_538701' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/538701?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵张仲宗感事</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_538701")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_538701_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_538701'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_538701'>诸侯救周衰，能事存笔削。<div id='poem_sentence_0_538701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_538701'>后学竞专门，肤引迷注脚。<div id='poem_sentence_1_538701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_538701'>宁知惧贼乱，诛意未为虐。<div id='poem_sentence_2_538701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_538701'>上皇志包荒，大度示恢廓。<div id='poem_sentence_3_538701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_538701'>误堕虏计中，九庙施箭凿。<div id='poem_sentence_4_538701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_538701'>将臣拥彊兵，首鼠事前却。<div id='poem_sentence_5_538701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_538701'>专雄怀顾望，散党失归着。<div id='poem_sentence_6_538701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_538701'>坐令两宫车，北辕狩沙漠。<div id='poem_sentence_7_538701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_538701'>天王绍绝统，愤此国势弱。<div id='poem_sentence_8_538701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_538701'>尝胆复大雠，此意良不薄。<div id='poem_sentence_9_538701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_538701'>向来督真奸，国典犹阔略。<div id='poem_sentence_10_538701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_538701'>群公争护前，循习久弥确。<div id='poem_sentence_11_538701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_538701'>黄屋泛沧溟，黔首寄矰缴。<div id='poem_sentence_12_538701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_538701'>世无管夷吾，老眼双泪阁。<div id='poem_sentence_13_538701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_538701'>何当诛赏行，浩叹成嗢噱。<div id='poem_sentence_14_538701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_538701'>曜灵还中天，冰雪自销铄。<div id='poem_sentence_15_538701_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_538701'></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_538701_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='326151815daf49928a57811064d98056_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("326151815daf49928a57811064d98056");'><span id='326151815daf49928a57811064d98056_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年</a>，49岁</div><div id='326151815daf49928a57811064d98056' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年1月</a>　正月，在德清，有文。作品：《湖州德清县重修孔子庙碑》<div id='poem_1233674' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233674' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233674?labeling=true' target='_blank'>湖州德清县重修孔子庙碑<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴四年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233674")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233674_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233674'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233674'>予少时尝闻诸长老言，吾邑初脱五季之乱，人乐更生，敦朴力穑，未知学也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233674_comment'></div>大中祥符间，予从祖书记始以儒学中进士甲科，名称籍甚，乡党荣之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233674_comment'></div>邑之子弟遂风劝于学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233674_comment'></div>其后正议大夫卢公父子踵取名第，翱翔要途，而学者日寖以盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233674_comment'></div>故有孔子庙，基下制狭，既不足以揭虔妥灵，而衿佩野逸，弗克群处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233674_comment'></div>迨明道壬申之岁，河南窦充来是邑，讯之卜人，以为馀不溪来自天目之山，注于邑之东南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233674_comment'></div>两山挟之，秀气横出，宜益有搢绅之祥，乃作今庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233674_comment'></div>直巽之隅，高明亢爽，非复旧比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233674_comment'></div>而文雅之士班班出焉，阀阅相望，若应厥卜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233674_comment'></div>予结发亦肄业其中，弦诵之声犹可想也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233674_comment'></div>中间朝廷兴学，而有司便事，仅于旧宇丹垩而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233674_comment'></div>然自初考卜，迄今百有三年，而墙屋颓圮，草茀于唐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233674_comment'></div>庙貌虽存，丹青缺落，使人喟然有宁不嗣音之叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1233674_comment'></div>春秋祀事，著于令甲，而器币牲牢之荐弗备弗蠲，神用不享。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1233674_comment'></div>太末郑如几隐居溪阴，一日过予曰：「吾侪儒服，顾不若佛老之徒严奉其祠，以侈大其师之说，耻也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1233674_comment'></div>已而率邑子沈良能相与告于邑令杨锬及凡境内之士大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1233674_comment'></div>士大夫悉劝趋之，争出缗钱以佐其费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1233674_comment'></div>乃尽彻去门庑，更立而一新之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1233674_comment'></div>面势隅落虽因其故，而栋楹显敞，视昔则又加焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1233674_comment'></div>爰即两庑析为斋庐以待学者，中严广殿，像设巍然，翼翼群公，绘事惟序，观者为之屏息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1233674_comment'></div>呜呼，休哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1233674_comment'></div>实经始于绍兴癸丑之仲冬，越明年春上丁行释奠之礼，落成焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1233674_comment'></div>是日也，予兄次律摄衣升堂，谈《春秋》大旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1233674_comment'></div>凡邑之士大夫济济在列，咸有肃容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1233674_comment'></div>邑令跽而请予文以记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1233674_comment'></div>予谓国家遭强胡之难，义士枕戈，武略是急，然未尝斯须忘右文之事，诚谓舍是则无以为天下也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1233674_comment'></div>吾邑令乃能閒抢攘之馀，导人所欲，立学崇祀，以夸四方，是可嘉已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1233674_comment'></div>乃为书其本末而系之以诗曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_1233674'>馀不之源，来自天目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1233674_comment'></div>注之两崖，其势若束。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1233674_comment'></div>惟邑东南，山萦水洑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1233674_comment'></div>始建庙宫，兹焉考卜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1233674_comment'></div>士也来游，文风载郁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1233674_comment'></div>更时抢攘，园蔬是鞠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1233674_comment'></div>岂其山川，秀气回复。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1233674_comment'></div>厥有吾徒，输金委粟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1233674_comment'></div>载新栋楹，工靡程督。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1233674_comment'></div>有神司之，不疾而速。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1233674_comment'></div>揭揭元圣，端冕衮服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1233674_comment'></div>群公从之，祀事孔肃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1233674_comment'></div>嗟我令尹，崇化表俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1233674_comment'></div>曰兴自躬，往继前躅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1233674_comment'></div>勉我士子，荒迨则辱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1233674_comment'></div>惟以嗣音，岂惟干禄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1233674_comment'></div>祥源泱泱，庶来其续。</div><div id='poem_sentence_43_1233674_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

开封（东京）

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1115&endYear=1115')">1115年3月23日</a>　在汴京，中何栗榜进士。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='ee5d267fbee9449595a33e0d692a6ff1_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ee5d267fbee9449595a33e0d692a6ff1");'><span id='ee5d267fbee9449595a33e0d692a6ff1_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年</a>　在汴京任太学录。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年7月4日</a>　在汴京任太学录。作贺启。作品：《贺湖守葛待制启》<div id='poem_1233616' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233616' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233616?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺湖守葛待制启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1122年7月4日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233616")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233616_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233616'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233616'>比审高牙，已临大府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233616_comment'></div>宽条一出，驩颂四驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233616_comment'></div>恭以某官心存古人，气盖当世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233616_comment'></div>名号一时之豪杰，学为四海之宗师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233616_comment'></div>两禁同游，最先德举；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233616_comment'></div>八科并中，岂止文鸣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233616_comment'></div>上心雅欲其居中，时论久嗟于补外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233616_comment'></div>然公卿皆惮，徒以君严之立朝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233616_comment'></div>而吏民不欺，亦赖长公之治郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233616_comment'></div>遂请便安之地，用苏疲瘵之氓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233616_comment'></div>正恐赐环，不容暖席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233616_comment'></div>某顷由弦诵，获进门墙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233616_comment'></div>服在下陈，方执簿书之役；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1233616_comment'></div>瞻言故国，莫修桑梓之恭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1233616_comment'></div>依向之成，倍万常品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1233616_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1233616_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1124')">1123-1124年</a>　在汴京任太学录。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年</a>　在汴京任太学博士。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年4月</a>　四月，金人破汴京。与求南下避难。<br /></div>

-----title
常州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='ad9bbe527f49431fba00e963583e8132_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ad9bbe527f49431fba00e963583e8132");'><span id='ad9bbe527f49431fba00e963583e8132_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1115&endYear=1117')">1115-1117年</a>，30-32岁</div><div id='ad9bbe527f49431fba00e963583e8132' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1115&endYear=1115')">1115年</a>　及第后，授濮阳县县学教授，以道远不便亲养，改常州州学教授，上谢启。作品：《谢改差常州学官启》<div id='poem_1233600' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233600' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233600?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢改差常州学官启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1115年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233600")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233600_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233600'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233600'>问涂湘水，方怀陟屺之思；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233600_comment'></div>易地兰陵，复预采芹之乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233600_comment'></div>幸既安于子职，喜遂发于亲颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233600_comment'></div>揣分云优，循涯以愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233600_comment'></div>伏念某天资梼昧，人品羁单。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233600_comment'></div>妄刻意于诗书，旋蹑踪于衿佩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233600_comment'></div>一随计牒，九换年华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233600_comment'></div>菘韭春秋，屡动故园之兴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233600_comment'></div>齑盐朝暮，贪观上国之光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233600_comment'></div>偶脱白丁，遽联黄甲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233600_comment'></div>洎亲荣三釜之禄，饰身叨五两之纶，谓寸进之可期，宜分阴之亦竞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233600_comment'></div>而乃赴铨十月，补吏一涯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233600_comment'></div>取道重江，念毛生之檄徒捧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1233600_comment'></div>待期荐岁，顾墨子之突未黔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1233600_comment'></div>敢图小物之私，曲缀大贤之念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1233600_comment'></div>达吁天之危悃，遂择地之初心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1233600_comment'></div>讫使便安，尽从愿欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1233600_comment'></div>兹盖某官恩深教载，德懋燮调。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1233600_comment'></div>推大钧之无垠，众由平进；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1233600_comment'></div>谓小人之有母，独轸深慈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1233600_comment'></div>便菽水之奉于近乡，脱风波之危于远役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1233600_comment'></div>矜怜若此，报称云何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1233600_comment'></div>某敢不激昂其衷，砥砺所学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1233600_comment'></div>庭闱爱日，已宽迟暮之怀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1233600_comment'></div>庠序承风，益广朋游之乐。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1233600_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1115&endYear=1115')">1115年</a>　攝归安尉，有谢启。作品：《谢运使差权知县事启》<div id='poem_1233595' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233595' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233595?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢运使差权知县事启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1115年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233595")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233595_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233595'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233595'>恭承邮报，俾摄县章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233595_comment'></div>调宓令之琴，焉知政理；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233595_comment'></div>拥毛生之檄，聊遂亲谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233595_comment'></div>蒙幸有馀，包羞无所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233595_comment'></div>伏念某嵚𡼭可笑，约结亡奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233595_comment'></div>懵学难成，顾短檠而自愧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233595_comment'></div>薄游寡偶，抚长铗以谁怜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233595_comment'></div>栖迟太学之十年，窃取奉常之一第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233595_comment'></div>尚须官次，伏处乡邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233595_comment'></div>谁是馈浆之人，空馀乞米之帖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233595_comment'></div>兹因弭节，方获曳裾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233595_comment'></div>擢于田里之中，寘在门墙之末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233595_comment'></div>公移远逮，就假一雷之封；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1233595_comment'></div>疾置惊传，亲著五云之字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1233595_comment'></div>顾惟凡琐，乃尔遭逢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1233595_comment'></div>此盖某官远业济时，高风励俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1233595_comment'></div>裕民足国，已操邦计之赢；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1233595_comment'></div>谪德量能，更欲人材之当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1233595_comment'></div>故令散吏，辄补旷官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1233595_comment'></div>某敢不勉尽所长，以待乃事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1233595_comment'></div>体一日葺居之戒，宁惮小劳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1233595_comment'></div>臻五月报政之期，庶收微效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1233595_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1233595_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1116&endYear=1116')">1116年</a>　在常州任州学教授。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1117&endYear=1117')">1117年3月</a>　在常州任州学教授。应盛公升之子庋请，作《朝请大夫盛公行状》。<div id='poem_1233673' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233673' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233673?labeling=true' target='_blank'>朝请大夫盛公行状</a><span class='authorDate'>（政和七年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233673")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233673_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233673'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233673'>曾祖得中，故不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233673_comment'></div>祖卞，故任漳州兵马监押，累赠右千牛卫大将军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233673_comment'></div>父侨，故任左朝奉大夫、直集贤院、知越州，累赠朝议大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233673_comment'></div>公讳允升，字德常，其先馀杭人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233673_comment'></div>公之四世祖蟠仕钱氏，爵位通显。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233673_comment'></div>钱氏举国内附，遂徙建德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233673_comment'></div>至集贤公，宦游吴兴，乐其山水，因家焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233673_comment'></div>公资禀端亮，自少小屏绝嬉弄，力学，问道古今，屹然如成人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233673_comment'></div>稍长，喜为文，辞采赡蔚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233673_comment'></div>一时贤士大夫咸称其能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233673_comment'></div>元丰间神宗皇帝辟上庠，以经术造天下士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233673_comment'></div>公挟其艺往试，率占上游，流辈多所降屈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233673_comment'></div>已而更元祐，尚声律，公自度雕琢之学，雅非所好，去之不复问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1233673_comment'></div>三年，哲宗皇帝亲郊，诏五品皆得官其子，遂以集贤公荫补太庙斋郎，调开封府酸枣县主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1233673_comment'></div>未赴，会集贤公捐舍馆，护丧归葬润州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1233673_comment'></div>即庐次，哀毁癯然，杖乃能起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1233673_comment'></div>卒丧，尉润之金坛，哀弗忘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1233673_comment'></div>秩满，奉太夫人还居吴兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1233673_comment'></div>属岁饥，盗斥境内，州将病之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1233673_comment'></div>先是乌程尉阙正员，檄公摄领，且语之盗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1233673_comment'></div>公分曹督捕，择所胁从，纵使缘亩，而执其渠首械送州，一境帖然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1233673_comment'></div>州上其事，司勋以格进官一等，丞苏之昆山县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1233673_comment'></div>崇宁元年官制行，授登仕郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1233673_comment'></div>公之丞于昆山也，事有便于民，无巨细辄举之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1233673_comment'></div>其非所便，不问久近，必去乃已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1233673_comment'></div>代有期，倾邑诣州泣留公再任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1233673_comment'></div>州不能夺，请于朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1233673_comment'></div>时上方建乡校、复里选，欲得能臣倚以办事，有旨从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1233673_comment'></div>邑旧有先圣庙，庳屋才数楹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1233673_comment'></div>公承诏一切更彻，根椽寸甓不歛于民，而落成先于诸郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1233673_comment'></div>部使者才之，联牍言上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1233673_comment'></div>三年，召至阙，改宣德郎、签判杭州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1233673_comment'></div>未几代回，摄开封府司刑曹事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1233673_comment'></div>尹辟公，真命且下，公独念太夫人春秋高，不乐北宦，丐还旧职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1233673_comment'></div>是时东平吕公惠卿帅杭，被旨择才吏，访境内逸迹，备修《九域图志》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1233673_comment'></div>杭于东南为大，诠次居多，帅难其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1233673_comment'></div>比公至，喜曰：「吾事办矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1233673_comment'></div>即一以属公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1233673_comment'></div>公搜抉无遗事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1233673_comment'></div>数月书成奏御，迁通直郎、通判扬州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1233673_comment'></div>大观二年，上躬受八宝，恩迁奉议郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1233673_comment'></div>往岁淮甸小歉，春秋二租及官所贷缗钱在民者，诏悉阁之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1233673_comment'></div>而强家大姓夤缘为奸，其非所应阁者诡免甚众，岁且丰，犹抵之不以给上事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1233673_comment'></div>公具簿最，句稽得实，谕使偿，凡为钱数十万以佐外计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1233673_comment'></div>迁朝奉郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1233673_comment'></div>太夫人寿且九十矣，念岁时姻族燕游之适，在官下，心未尝一日忘吴兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1233673_comment'></div>公惕然曰：「吾始以亲故仕，今所居非亲所好，虽食万钱，谊不忍」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1233673_comment'></div>即解印韨致其事以归左右，就养惟谨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1233673_comment'></div>居无何，太夫人以寿终，公执丧如集贤公时，益不懈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1233673_comment'></div>政和二年，当路以公年未艾，才不宜遂休，表复用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1233673_comment'></div>训词褒许，即以旧领阶官司开封府户曹事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1233673_comment'></div>方朝廷考正徵角二声，庶燕乐以釐革郑卫淫哇之习。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1233673_comment'></div>公上所著《乐书》数万言，论辨古乐，所以析用中正之法甚悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1233673_comment'></div>上嘉用之，改仪曹兼大晟府制造官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1233673_comment'></div>三年，司勋奏公曩摄邑苏之常熟，捕获盗铸金钱，法应赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1233673_comment'></div>由是累迁朝请郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1233673_comment'></div>九月燕乐成，上命辅臣覆视，唯公所制精妙一时，特恩迁朝奉大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1233673_comment'></div>踰月，赐服三品，皆异数也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1233673_comment'></div>四年，营奉明达皇后寝园，与有劳，迁朝散大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1233673_comment'></div>俄得请知秀州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1233673_comment'></div>五年，公犹待次乡郡，以大晟奏功，迁朝请大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1233673_comment'></div>一日，忽语所亲曰：「始吾乞身强健，自谓终老里门，渠意及此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1233673_comment'></div>今而归，冞足以侈上恩，可但已邪」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1233673_comment'></div>因复请休于家，理别圃苕霅之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1233673_comment'></div>幅巾藜杖，往来其间，澹乎若与世无营者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1233673_comment'></div>阅秘典日数百纸，要以了达死生，人亦初未之知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1233673_comment'></div>居数月感疾，命诸子具秘器，卜寿藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1233673_comment'></div>既，乃曰：「后事豫矣，瞑目何憾」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1233673_comment'></div>即折简素所从游，告以逝日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1233673_comment'></div>至日，终于正寝，治命不乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1233673_comment'></div>其悟解乃如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1233673_comment'></div>实政和六年闰正月十八日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1233673_comment'></div>公雅有策画，临事不为苟且之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1233673_comment'></div>所至绩效蔼然，有闻于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1233673_comment'></div>故所迁官率繇懋赏，独于荣利恬静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1233673_comment'></div>比再挂冠，年犹未衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1233673_comment'></div>南州士大夫高其行，爱慕在色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1233673_comment'></div>使公彷徉以进，则其所施设何如哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1233673_comment'></div>享年五十有八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1233673_comment'></div>娶孙氏，封宜人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1233673_comment'></div>子男六人：曰康，迪功郎、婺州兵曹掾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1233673_comment'></div>曰庋，迪功郎、坊州司刑曹事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1233673_comment'></div>曰庚、庠、庶、序，皆游乡校，为儒生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1233673_comment'></div>女七人：长适登仕郎朱德延，次适迪功郎钱均，次适贡士陈琦，次适贡士吴景信，次适太学博士钱圻，馀尚幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1233673_comment'></div>孙男一人，女二人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1233673_comment'></div>明年三月十四日，诸孤奉公之柩葬于乌程县九元乡金盖山之原，先所卜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1233673_comment'></div>某与公实同里，而公之子庋疏其治行属于不腆之文，且曰：「将求名世道德君子铭焉，以图不朽」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1233673_comment'></div>谨叙次于右端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1233673_comment'></div>谨状。</div><div id='poem_sentence_88_1233673_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
嘉兴
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='7d03e42c96874a7ca139ec9bca4bee2b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7d03e42c96874a7ca139ec9bca4bee2b");'><span id='7d03e42c96874a7ca139ec9bca4bee2b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1118&endYear=1118')">1118年</a>，33岁</div><div id='7d03e42c96874a7ca139ec9bca4bee2b' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在秀州任司兵曹事兼推勘公事。秀守苗郎中荐其改官，上谢启。作品：《谢秀守苗郎中举改官启》<div id='poem_1233620' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233620' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233620?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢秀守苗郎中举改官启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1118年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233620")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233620_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233620'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233620'>二纪服儒，犹念呻吟之旧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233620_comment'></div>一官书狱，岂堪流落之馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233620_comment'></div>遽辱提撕，重为荣耀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233620_comment'></div>伏念某受生多难，涉世少徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233620_comment'></div>偶从钟釜之谋，辄污轩裳之列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233620_comment'></div>衒玉贾石，夫岂本心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233620_comment'></div>乞酒得浆，亦其定分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233620_comment'></div>亟舍弦歌之乐，骤亲敲扑之烦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233620_comment'></div>群言譊譊，争沮幕中之辩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233620_comment'></div>独行踽踽，敢矜席上之珍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233620_comment'></div>乃使挂需头之章，终免为摇尾之态。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233620_comment'></div>静言特达，重愧空疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233620_comment'></div>此盖伏遇某官隐德在时，深忠许国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1233620_comment'></div>牧人驭众，共师循吏之风流；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1233620_comment'></div>推贤与能，自得上臣之识度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1233620_comment'></div>优容寒素，曲赐奖成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1233620_comment'></div>某敢不铭肌感恩，刻意为善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1233620_comment'></div>庸庸末学，傥有见于施为；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1233620_comment'></div>断断馀生，庶无忘于报称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1233620_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1233620_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在秀州任司兵曹事兼推勘公事。作品：《次韵秀守苗郎中喜雨》《秀州馆交代乐语》<div id='poem_538755' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_538755' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/538755?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵秀守苗郎中喜雨</a><span class='authorDate'>（1118年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_538755'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_538755'>旌旆传呼起伏龙，雨翻枯泽已全通。<div id='poem_sentence_0_538755_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_538755'>招呼急吹添秋思，袪逐骄阳助岁功。<div id='poem_sentence_1_538755_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_538755'>蝝子有知先避境<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：邻境多旱蝗。）</span>，葑根无着尽浮空。<div id='poem_sentence_2_538755_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_538755'>老农自笑豚蹄祝，惠政流行盍屡丰。<div id='poem_sentence_3_538755_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_538755'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_538755_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_538979' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_538979' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/538979?labeling=true' target='_blank'>秀州馆交代乐语口号</a><span class='authorDate'>（1118年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_538979")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_538979_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_538979'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_538979'>一麾相望继芳尘，召杜风流主与宾。<div id='poem_sentence_0_538979_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_538979'>芸阁去方思就日，竹符来及趁班春。<div id='poem_sentence_1_538979_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_538979'>清谈款密看论旧，善政从容许告新。<div id='poem_sentence_2_538979_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_538979'>早晚银台双诏下，共期持橐侍严宸<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上同上书卷一一）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_538979_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_538979'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_538979_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
杭州
-----detail

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年10月</a>　十月，避难至杭州。始与曾惇游。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='1a2b51af49cb48259f7d5e5bee81fae6_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年1月20日</a>　正月二十日，在临安。迁御史中丞。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年1月</a>　上辞免状。作品：《辞免除御史中丞奏状》<div id='poem_1233505' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233505' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233505?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免除御史中丞奏状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233505")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233505_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233505'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233505'>右，臣伏蒙圣恩，除臣御史中丞，日下供职者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233505_comment'></div>闻命震惊，罔知所措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233505_comment'></div>窃以中执法之任，是为三独坐之联。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233505_comment'></div>所以镇肃百僚，纲纪万事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233505_comment'></div>侍赤墀而簪笔，参陪顾问之荣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233505_comment'></div>剡白简而飞章，总领弹诃之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233505_comment'></div>不有宿望，曷副超除？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233505_comment'></div>伏念臣门族寒微，性资昏懵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233505_comment'></div>徒以顷从末路，骤对清光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233505_comment'></div>一言偶合于圣聪，三院遍叨于亲擢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233505_comment'></div>天地之恩至大，不敢谋身；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233505_comment'></div>蝼蚁之生甚微，唯知许国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233505_comment'></div>中缘狂妄，自速罪辜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1233505_comment'></div>方怀绂而返故乡，俄赐环而归旧列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1233505_comment'></div>既踰累月，奚补万分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1233505_comment'></div>仰负睿知，理宜投劾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1233505_comment'></div>尝陈危悃，意欲祈閒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1233505_comment'></div>敢图宸眷之益加，亟置台端而躐进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1233505_comment'></div>臣之自揣，实不能胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1233505_comment'></div>傥或贪冒宠私，俯偻拜命，则必重增尤累，满溢兴灾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1233505_comment'></div>岂唯咈于师言，诚恐堕于国体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1233505_comment'></div>伏望陛下特回渊听，追寝误恩，改授真贤，以安素分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1233505_comment'></div>臣下情无任恳祈迫切之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1233505_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1233505_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年1月</a>　上自代状。作品：《除御史中丞举左司员外郎潘良贵自代状》<div id='poem_1233506' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233506' id='poem_title_1233506_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233506'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233506'>伏睹某官才周学富，行峻识明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233506_comment'></div>考治乱之端，智略通于国体；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233506_comment'></div>辩邪正之分，忠言切于人情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233506_comment'></div>出入十年，始终一节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233506_comment'></div>声称望实，臣所不如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233506_comment'></div>举以代臣，实允公议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233506_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233506_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1233506_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年1月</a>　是月，在临安。论朝廷当掌兵权、修兵政，以成中兴之势。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年2月</a>　二月，在临安。奏徐端本、赵公竤等人为官猥滥，乞罢之；奏请高宗斥还刘光世所献缯帛方物；请置史官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年3月</a>　三月，在临安。奏请高宗明示好恶，斥徐康国而焚其所献金屏障等物。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年闰4月6日</a>　闰四月初六，在临安。劾李弥大谋间君臣、怀私耽宠，乞降黜之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年5月</a>　五月，在临安。奏徐天民掊克蠹民之罪。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年5月21日</a>　五月二十一日，在临安。推言灾异，请高宗行事必以诚。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年5月24日</a>　五月二十四日，在临安。奏请于石港料角等处存养水手，以备海防。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年6月21日</a>　六月二十一日，在临安，奏请许馆职兼在京厘务官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年6月23日</a>　六月二十三日，在临安，草诏书。作品：《赐参知政事孟庾辞免通议大夫恩命不允诏》《再赐孟庾辞免不允诏》<div id='poem_1233420' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233420' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233420?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐参知政事孟庾辞免通议大夫恩命不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年6月23日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233420")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233420_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233420'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233420'>朕以闽越湖湘之间大憝逋诛，根连蔓结，胁我赤子，盗弄库兵，宿师连年，未克平殄，眷然南顾，实疚于怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233420_comment'></div>乃辍帷幄之臣，而总干戈之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233420_comment'></div>卿义形于色，慷慨请行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233420_comment'></div>揆策投机，指授诸将。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233420_comment'></div>群凶随以荡灭，数路为之肃清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233420_comment'></div>坐使黎元，复见休息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233420_comment'></div>论功甚茂，朌赏犹轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233420_comment'></div>时惟股肱，必识朕意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233420_comment'></div>抗章避宠，岂所望焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233420_comment'></div>夫谦冲之节虽云可尚，令出而寝，卿岂不为朝廷惜乎！</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1233420_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1233421' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233421' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233421?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再赐孟庾辞免不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年6月23日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233421")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233421_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233421'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233421'>朕比遣师徒，往平寇盗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233421_comment'></div>想山川之悠远，爰念怀归；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233421_comment'></div>悯臣下之勤劳，岂忘劝赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233421_comment'></div>矧我哲辅，夙有壮图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233421_comment'></div>入则参与政机，谋谟足以决大议；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233421_comment'></div>出则总提师律，精神足以折遐冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233421_comment'></div>蠢兹啸聚之群，讵费坐筹之画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233421_comment'></div>指顾而定，逋逃一空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233421_comment'></div>歌《杕杜》之诗，士方休舍；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233421_comment'></div>变潢池之习，民乃奠居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233421_comment'></div>褒律肆行，需章荐至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233421_comment'></div>载惟谦抑，殊咈眷怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233421_comment'></div>夫位高而志卑，固云美矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1233421_comment'></div>功多者赏厚，犹用歉然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1233421_comment'></div>往其钦承，勿复固请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1233421_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1233421_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年6月28日</a>　六月二十八日，在临安，辟施锯为御史台主簿。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年7月28日</a>　七月二十八日，在临安。试吏部尚书，兼权翰林学士。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年7月</a>　上辞免状。作品：《辞免除吏部尚书奏状》《辞免兼权翰林学士奏状》<div id='poem_1233507' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233507' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233507?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免除吏部尚书奏状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233507")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233507_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233507'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233507'>右，臣伏准尚书省劄子，奉圣旨，除臣吏部尚书兼权翰林学士，日下供职者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233507_comment'></div>闻命震惊，罔知所措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233507_comment'></div>窃以天官六卿之长，铨综人物，地极高华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233507_comment'></div>祖宗以来，惟是询求一时硕德宿望之士，命使居之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233507_comment'></div>故夷夏知名，搢绅动色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233507_comment'></div>朝廷之上，自然尊荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233507_comment'></div>就非其才，宁若虚次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233507_comment'></div>傥缘恩眷，轻以假人，公言沸腾，必至累国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233507_comment'></div>况复兼官翰墨，备极政事文章之选，尤不可不慎也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233507_comment'></div>伏念臣迂愚朴拙，一无寸长，遭遇圣明，误叨器使，待罪言路，首尾四年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233507_comment'></div>虽有拳拳爱君之心，祇罄孤忠，不为身计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233507_comment'></div>然智识凡下，昧于几微，何补事功，徒积仇怨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233507_comment'></div>仰恃日月之照，幽隐必临，直道径行，不避谗谤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1233507_comment'></div>终缘思虑过当，气血衰残，涉秋以来，十日九病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1233507_comment'></div>适以迫近防虞之际，未敢祈閒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1233507_comment'></div>遽蒙圣恩，横加庸品，超躐众俊，并冒宠除。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1233507_comment'></div>在臣之愚，岂遑安处？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1233507_comment'></div>况臣少时学为场屋之文，随众觅举，既忝禄仕，旧学已忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1233507_comment'></div>白简之词不拘音节，尚犹牵彊累日，仅乃成章，退省荒疏，常怀跼蹐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1233507_comment'></div>今复假之禁林之直，尤非所堪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1233507_comment'></div>阁笔含毫，何以塞责？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1233507_comment'></div>不免披沥血诚，仰干君父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1233507_comment'></div>伏望陛下特轸天慈，追还成命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1233507_comment'></div>除臣一在外宫观差遣，俾遂小休，以安素分，不胜幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1233507_comment'></div>臣卑情无任祈天望圣激切屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1233507_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1233507_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1233508' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233508' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233508?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免兼权翰林学士奏状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233508")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233508_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233508'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233508'>右，臣近蒙恩除前件差遣，寻具辞免，仍乞改除一在外宫观，伏奉诏书，不允所乞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233508_comment'></div>恭读圣训，感涕交流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233508_comment'></div>窃念臣奋繇寒素，初无寸长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233508_comment'></div>曲被神圣之知，叨尘耳目之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233508_comment'></div>虽尽言不识忌讳，每荷包容；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233508_comment'></div>然孤立不为比周，终虞颠覆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233508_comment'></div>今者误恩遽及，二组兼纡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233508_comment'></div>在臣之愚，岂克胜任？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233508_comment'></div>而搢绅留滞之久，文籍散亡之馀，铨总失宜，上下交病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233508_comment'></div>使臣夙夜殚竭驽蹇，犹恐不足以办此一职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233508_comment'></div>至于禁林之选，翰墨是司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233508_comment'></div>当此多故之时，凡下诏令，必欲鬯达圣意，感动人心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233508_comment'></div>自非老于文学之人，孰宜居此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1233508_comment'></div>而臣术业空疏，语言拙涩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1233508_comment'></div>文章体制，既非素习，加以忧深感疾，福过挻灾，志气凋零，旧学都废，驱之就职，必误使令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1233508_comment'></div>不免再沥血诚，仰干宸造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1233508_comment'></div>所有铨总之职，臣惧再三之渎，不敢更具恳辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1233508_comment'></div>惟是兼权翰林学士，实非微臣所当冒处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1233508_comment'></div>伏望天慈特回渊听，追寝施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1233508_comment'></div>不唯于臣愚分得以自安，在朝廷因任之际，舍短用长，责其实效，不胜幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1233508_comment'></div>臣无任祈天望圣激切屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1233508_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1233508_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年7月</a>　上自代状。作品：《除吏部尚书举左朝奉大夫直龙图阁辛炳自代状》<div id='poem_1233509' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233509' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233509?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除吏部尚书举左朝奉大夫直龙图阁辛炳自代状</a><span class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233509'>伏睹某官学有渊源，行无瑕玷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233509_comment'></div>恢闳之略，足以济时；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233509_comment'></div>赡蔚之文，足以华国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233509_comment'></div>恬静介洁，名重东南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233509_comment'></div>举以代臣，实允公议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233509_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233509_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1233509_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年9月9日</a>　九月初九，在临安，以吏部尚书兼权翰林学士兼侍读。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年9月</a>　上辞免状。作品：《辞免侍读奏状》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年9月16日</a>　九月十六日，在临安，乞诏礼官以他字代渊圣御名。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年9月18日</a>　九月十八日，在临安，草诏书。作品：《赐新除翰林学士知制诰綦崇礼辞免恩命不允诏》<div id='poem_1233422' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233422' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233422?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐新除翰林学士知制诰綦崇礼辞免恩命不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年9月18日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233422")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233422_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233422'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233422'>朕纂承丕图，戡定多难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233422_comment'></div>将欲德意志虑鬯达乎斯民，盖在号令文章鼓动乎当世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233422_comment'></div>翰墨之选，兹惟艰哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233422_comment'></div>卿学穷本原，文备体要，代予述作，亦既有年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233422_comment'></div>再隶职于卿曹，复兼官于辞禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233422_comment'></div>演纶滋久，摛藻益工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233422_comment'></div>报淮南之书，卿其视草而遣矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233422_comment'></div>下山东之诏，民将扶杖而听之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233422_comment'></div>肆加即拜之恩，示予亲擢之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233422_comment'></div>奚为逊避，犹徇故常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233422_comment'></div>宜副佥谐之言，往就久虚之次。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1233422_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年9月19日</a>　九月十九日，在临安，行制文。作品：《除郭仲荀武泰军节度使依前侍卫亲军步军都指挥使权主管殿前司公事制》<div id='poem_1233417' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233417' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233417?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除郭仲荀武泰军节度使依前侍卫亲军步军都指挥使权主管殿前司公事制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年9月19日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233417")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233417_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233417'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233417'>门下：胜负者兵家之常，将帅莫先于贾勇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233417_comment'></div>予夺者国柄之大，帝王尤厚于植恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233417_comment'></div>眷我阃臣，丽于邦典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233417_comment'></div>解斋旄而兹久，扈岩陛以弥勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233417_comment'></div>爰因霈音，式朌涣号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233417_comment'></div>具官郭仲荀资禀沈毅，节槩轩昂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233417_comment'></div>风流绍于故家，气略闻于殊域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233417_comment'></div>训齐士卒，适程李宽猛之宜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233417_comment'></div>保障疆陲，合孙吴擒纵之要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233417_comment'></div>战阀屡上，勋盟孔昭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233417_comment'></div>自从朕于艰虞，更饬身于忠谨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233417_comment'></div>属虏骑饮江而南下，虑敌人并海而东侵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233417_comment'></div>授以偏师，扼其要路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1233417_comment'></div>兵势弗竞，避地踰一舍之遥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1233417_comment'></div>物论既腾，启途收六纛之峻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1233417_comment'></div>顷召还于裔土，旋典司于禁兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1233417_comment'></div>谋谟慨然，仪观伟甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1233417_comment'></div>念世类之祥未艾，知功名之志不衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1233417_comment'></div>将励山西之劲臣，遂付黔南之巨镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1233417_comment'></div>周庐徼道，总中尉之八屯；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1233417_comment'></div>锡盾彫戈，复元戎之十乘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1233417_comment'></div>兹为宠渥，庸示眷私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1233417_comment'></div>于乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1233417_comment'></div>伏波迟留，克成铜柱之略；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1233417_comment'></div>营平慎重，愿上金城之图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1233417_comment'></div>傥无愧于古人，盍有为于当世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1233417_comment'></div>往复休命，益励壮猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1233417_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1233417_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年9月30日</a>　九月三十日，在临安，草诏书。作品：《赐新除庆远军节度使克醴泉观使特封徳清县开国子食邑五百户食实封二百户邢焕辞免恩命不允诏》《再赐邢焕辞免不允断来章诏》<div id='poem_1233428' class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233428'>朕会朝方岳，竣事合宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233428_comment'></div>告宗祀之备成，遍敷惠泽；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233428_comment'></div>念后家之流落，未启戚藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233428_comment'></div>颇采彝章，诚为阙典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233428_comment'></div>自椒涂正长秋之位，属翟驭从朔方之行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233428_comment'></div>感此伤心，居焉累岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233428_comment'></div>推朕怀两宫之意，彼岂忘亲；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233428_comment'></div>广朕加四海之恩，兹为笃近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233428_comment'></div>爰设将旄之重，肆开帅阃之雄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233428_comment'></div>匪朕所私，繄国之旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233428_comment'></div>曷形逊牍，犹避宠名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233428_comment'></div>况卿谦厚律身，忠谨事上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233428_comment'></div>万里归于逆旅，谅险阻之备更；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1233428_comment'></div>五载服于故官，亦靖共之足尚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1233428_comment'></div>孚号既发，佥言允谐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1233428_comment'></div>勿复徇于劳谦，其往承于茂渥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1233428_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1233428_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1233429' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233429' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233429?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再赐邢焕辞免不允断来章诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年9月30日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233429'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233429'>朕追考祖宗之旧，凡建节旄之雄，自非勋德之优，用为报称，必以宗姻之懿，昭其宠荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233429_comment'></div>卿世为德门，居有贤誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233429_comment'></div>以儒臣之英而识通机秘，以后父之贵而志绝豪华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233429_comment'></div>熙事备成，惠术遍举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233429_comment'></div>联长安之戚里，所存几人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233429_comment'></div>开庆远之帅藩，姑循彝制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233429_comment'></div>其往承于异渥，毋曲徇于牢辞。</div><div
