showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233453?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐邢焕除庆远军节度使充醴泉观使辞免恩命不允口宣</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年9月30日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233453")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233453_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233453'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233453'>卿系出儒家，恩联戚里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233453_comment'></div>谦恭有守，静慎无哗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233453_comment'></div>斋钺既朌，廷绅允穆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233453_comment'></div>往承茂渥，勿复牢辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233453_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1233453_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年10月</a>　十月，在临安。以黄策之子请，为其父作墓志铭。作品：《黄直阁墓志铭》<div id='poem_1233676' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233676' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233676?labeling=true' target='_blank'>黄直阁墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴二年十月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233676")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233676_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233676'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233676'>秘阁黄君子虚殁，既葬，诸孤丧服更造予，跣以泣曰：「先君子葬未克铭，治命以属公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233676_comment'></div>不肖孤其忍废先君子之命？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233676_comment'></div>敢碣墓以请」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233676_comment'></div>予与君雅故，且诸孤请益急，则诺而铭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233676_comment'></div>君讳策，子虚其字也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233676_comment'></div>其先居建之浦城，为望族，世有彻官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233676_comment'></div>自大父游姑苏，乐其土俗，因家焉，今为姑苏人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233676_comment'></div>曾大父浃累赠奉议郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233676_comment'></div>大父挺仕承议郎，累赠金紫光禄大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233676_comment'></div>父彦仕朝奉大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233676_comment'></div>君性豪迈，风神峻拔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233676_comment'></div>方童丱时，出语已惊人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233676_comment'></div>弱冠一举进士中乙科，追和梁昭明所选诗，持见眉山苏公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1233676_comment'></div>公期之曰：「异时必以文显」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1233676_comment'></div>初选授杭州司理参军，折狱精明，吏屏息不敢弄以事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1233676_comment'></div>秩满，授开封府雍丘县主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1233676_comment'></div>元符末，诏许中外言事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1233676_comment'></div>是时昭慈圣献皇后既复位号，而典册有未尽正者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1233676_comment'></div>君上书引古义争之，言剧剀切，藉藉闻搢绅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1233676_comment'></div>荐者以君才磊落，不宜浮沉簿领，改授齐州州学教谕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1233676_comment'></div>会崇宁党锢之论起，故老名臣鲜克免者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1233676_comment'></div>君亦坐前所上书刻名党石，羁置登州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1233676_comment'></div>二年，徙海州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1233676_comment'></div>既而上皇感寤，斥用事大臣，破党论，仆其石立碎之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1233676_comment'></div>君例还姑苏休官，自号随缘居士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1233676_comment'></div>闭户读书，益自刻苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1233676_comment'></div>为文章瑰词老气，络绎间起，至其甚得意，视古作者无愧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1233676_comment'></div>佳时胜日，相羊山水间，赋诗自娱，澹乎若与世无营。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1233676_comment'></div>如是二十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1233676_comment'></div>故礼部侍郎邹公浩、谏议大夫刘公安世、右司员外郎陈公瓘，皆以敢谏争名重当世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1233676_comment'></div>君从之游，上下其议论，相厚善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1233676_comment'></div>宣和中，姑苏守贾諲知君名，强欲吏之，辟致幕下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1233676_comment'></div>诸有势人，意君可撼以禄，争为出力推挽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1233676_comment'></div>龃龉不合，去为浙西提举司干办公事，移京东，改发运司主管文字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1233676_comment'></div>君亦未尝薄其官，所居称治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1233676_comment'></div>上即位之二年，改宣教郎、通判严州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1233676_comment'></div>明年召对行在所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1233676_comment'></div>又明年，上追录党人，除直秘阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1233676_comment'></div>其在严州，数以争可否忤部使者意，使者嫉之，诬劾君纵狱事，按验无所得，卒夺一官，左受宣义郎罢去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1233676_comment'></div>退而筑室五湖之旁，日阅浮屠氏书，要以刮去世故、捐爱憎，然其了达，乃于死生之际，脱然如去来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1233676_comment'></div>忽一旦起盥栉，呼诸子侍前，曰：「吾其脱于斯乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1233676_comment'></div>而辈行自力，毋坠吾训」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1233676_comment'></div>语讫，危坐而逝，实绍兴二年八月十有二日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1233676_comment'></div>享年六十有三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1233676_comment'></div>娶程氏，生三男：曰维、曰缨、曰纵、皆以儒业世其家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1233676_comment'></div>一女，适从事郎胡总。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1233676_comment'></div>君作寿冢于灵岩之麓，手植之木拱矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1233676_comment'></div>诸孤即以其年十月十日举君之柩葬焉，从其卜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1233676_comment'></div>先是，君得元符词臣手疏，载上皇圣训，备言昭慈之复位号，乃钦圣追用泰陵悔意，惊且喜曰：「天也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1233676_comment'></div>使泰陵之意白于天下，死不恨」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1233676_comment'></div>亟上之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1233676_comment'></div>君既殁，始用昭慈戚属信安郡王忠厚奏请，诏以其疏付史官，示万世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1233676_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1233676_comment'></div>君才百于人而不一试，偲偲然为国纳忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1233676_comment'></div>虽摈斥流落以终其身，不少悔，其亦可哀也已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1233676_comment'></div>有文集百二十卷藏于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1233676_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_56_1233676'>山盘盘兮，松桂萧森。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1233676_comment'></div>川渺渺兮，鱼龙啸吟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1233676_comment'></div>顾瞻中丘兮，宛其幽深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1233676_comment'></div>曰惟哲人之藏兮，抱器陆沈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1233676_comment'></div>讯来世兮，谁其赏音。</div><div id='poem_sentence_60_1233676_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年11月17日</a>　十一月十七日，在临安，奏捕贼酬赏事宜。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年11月20日</a>　十一月二十日，在临安，奏乞将八路阙令吏部借使差注。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年12月8日</a>　十二月初八，在临安。以李纲罢，除龙图阁学士、湖南安抚使，兼知潭州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年12月</a>　上辞免状。作品：《乞罢除龙图阁学士荆湖南路安抚使兼知潭州奏状》<div id='poem_1233511' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233511' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233511?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞罢除龙图阁学士荆湖南路安抚使兼知潭州奏状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233511")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233511_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233511'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233511'>右，臣今月八日准尚书省劄子，奉圣旨除臣龙图阁学士、充荆湖南路安抚使、兼知潭州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233511_comment'></div>闻命震惊，罔知所措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233511_comment'></div>臣窃谓国家多事之际，固非臣子惜身之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233511_comment'></div>而况河图峻职，湘潭会府，宠命并至，于臣甚荣，义当驰驱，即日引道，岂宜自列，复有所言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233511_comment'></div>然臣有一介拳拳孤危之虑，不敢不控告于君父之前者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233511_comment'></div>臣顷自疏远，误被眷怜，亟从小官，遍历言路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233511_comment'></div>初无左右先容之助，尽出圣神特达之知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233511_comment'></div>故于军旅之事，素非思虑所及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233511_comment'></div>比来或闻湖南残寇尚复啸聚，而臣猥以弱材，骤当重寄，必致败事，万无可疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233511_comment'></div>兼臣自荷擢用，以言为职，于今累年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233511_comment'></div>而臣天资戆愚，志在展尽，每荷天语慰勉，许赐保全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233511_comment'></div>不避怨仇，实恃陛下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233511_comment'></div>臣犹过虑，数丐退閒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1233511_comment'></div>未报大恩，尚啬其去，臣亦累尝奏禀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1233511_comment'></div>止缘秋冬防虞之日，未敢力为妨贤之请；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1233511_comment'></div>而又私门祸患，病骨零丁，皆俟初春，尽当控诉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1233511_comment'></div>非臣今日创为此言，若冒选除，不自量力，虽杀臣身，何补国事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1233511_comment'></div>伏望圣慈终始哀怜，罢臣今来所除职名，与一在外宫观，使得休养疾病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1233511_comment'></div>傥臣未填沟壑，犹冀他日万一勉彊，以报殊私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1233511_comment'></div>冒渎天听，臣无任祈哀请命激切屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1233511_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1233511_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年12月</a>　上自代状。作品：《除龙图阁学士举左奉议郎莫仲珪自代状》<div id='poem_1233512' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233512' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233512?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除龙图阁学士举左奉议郎莫仲圭自代状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233512")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233512_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233512'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233512'>伏睹某官学问淹该，操行纯洁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233512_comment'></div>望实之美，见推士林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233512_comment'></div>举以代臣，实允公议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233512_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233512_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1233512_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年12月13日</a>　十二月十三日，在临安。力辞湖南之命，遂命改知常州。复以疾辞，改提举江州太平观。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='a1a9d35a4d134d389e8adb6b58428f33_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a1a9d35a4d134d389e8adb6b58428f33");'><span id='a1a9d35a4d134d389e8adb6b58428f33_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年</a>，49岁</div><div id='a1a9d35a4d134d389e8adb6b58428f33' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年7月</a>　上谢表。作品：《谢除吏部尚书表》<div id='poem_1233483' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233483' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233483?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢除吏部尚书表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233483")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233483_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233483'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233483'>拥麾临郡，靡闻治状之优；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233483_comment'></div>曳履还朝，忽拜召音之迅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233483_comment'></div>班联虽旧，眷渥弥新<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233483_comment'></div>伏念臣奋迹孤生，受知明主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233483_comment'></div>越从羁旅之次，寘在英游之閒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233483_comment'></div>六年于兹，一节以守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233483_comment'></div>犯颜狂论，仰翳全度之容；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233483_comment'></div>率意妄行，频触骇机之发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233483_comment'></div>顷违表著，退即丘樊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233483_comment'></div>庶少避于满盈，亦苟逃于罪戾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233483_comment'></div>恩缘谋帅，诏使牧民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233483_comment'></div>虽公家之利无不为，粗识所向；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233483_comment'></div>然军旅之事未之学，终愧斯言，曾坐席之未温，已赐环之亟下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1233483_comment'></div>自惊衰朽，重历禁严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1233483_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下信顺尚贤，聪明稽古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1233483_comment'></div>多士杂遝，皆洞照其肺肝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1233483_comment'></div>群胡跳梁，已阴得其要领。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1233483_comment'></div>将开兴运，并用旧人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1233483_comment'></div>如臣等夷，亦在比数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1233483_comment'></div>臣敢不激昂于事，洗涤其衷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1233483_comment'></div>涉世蹈忧患之途，其身已老；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1233483_comment'></div>报君持忠义之节，此志不移。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1233483_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年8月21日</a>　八月二十一日，在临安。以吏部尚书兼权翰林学士。上辞免札子。作品：《辞免除兼翰林学士札子》<div id='poem_1233518' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233518' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233518?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免除兼翰林学士劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年8月21日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233518")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233518_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233518'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233518'>右，臣今月二十二日准尚书省劄子，奉圣旨除臣兼翰林学士者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233518_comment'></div>闻命震惊，罔知所措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233518_comment'></div>臣伏见侍从之列被旨兼权他职多矣，例不敢辄有辞免者，恐涉避事之嫌也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233518_comment'></div>惟是翰墨之林，儒臣高选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233518_comment'></div>供奉述作，既专代于王言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233518_comment'></div>燕见咨询，实与闻于国论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233518_comment'></div>兼官寓直，尤当择才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233518_comment'></div>而臣已试无状，不敢再冒恩除，辄忘此嫌，引义自列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233518_comment'></div>重念臣本以田野之质，学为场屋之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233518_comment'></div>音节疾徐，初非素习；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233518_comment'></div>体制高下，焉能彊知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233518_comment'></div>昨者迫于威命之严，黾勉兼摄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233518_comment'></div>辞气卑弱，无以鬯达德意之精微，传播四方，诚恐累国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1233518_comment'></div>矧以连年忧患，心志凋零，口耳所传，尽皆废忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1233518_comment'></div>加又铨衡剧曹，案牍填委，稍稽拨遣，动致烦言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1233518_comment'></div>夙夜究心，犹惧不逮，傥或冒宠贪荣，复兼两职，才力不副，旷败无疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1233518_comment'></div>纵蒙陛下保全，未加诛斥，而臣之私分何以自安？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1233518_comment'></div>伏望圣慈察臣所沥悃诚，出于迫切，特赐追还成命，改授能臣，庶几臣之短拙获免自暴，实为幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1233518_comment'></div>干冒天威，臣无任战灼之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1233518_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1233518_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年9月28日</a>　九月二十八日，在临安。以吏部尚书兼权翰林学士迁中大夫，除参知政事。上辞免表。作品：《辞免除参知政事表》<div id='poem_1233485' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233485' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233485?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免除参知政事表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年9月28日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233485")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233485_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233485'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233485'>任重人微，敢殚危悃；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233485_comment'></div>恩隆命确，未锡俞音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233485_comment'></div>更陈迫切之辞，仰渎盖高之听<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233485_comment'></div>伏念臣章句之学，拙于济时；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233485_comment'></div>田野之资，昧于谋国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233485_comment'></div>徒以四海至孤之迹，曲荷九重特达之知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233485_comment'></div>遍历高华，曾微补发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233485_comment'></div>比膺召命，复长铨曹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233485_comment'></div>方日俟于谴诃，遽参陪于机政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233485_comment'></div>况风尘之警未息，郊垒滋多；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233485_comment'></div>而宵旰之虑益深，朝纲犹紊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233485_comment'></div>柬求误及，称塞愈难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233485_comment'></div>伏望皇帝陛下遍察猷为，先求望实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1233485_comment'></div>公回宸渥，别授时英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1233485_comment'></div>虽独智之有临，宅心奚隐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1233485_comment'></div>苟众听之无咈，反汗何嫌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1233485_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1233485_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年9月</a>　上辞免札子。作品：《辞免除参知政事札子》<div id='poem_1233519' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233519' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233519?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免除参知政事劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233519")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233519_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233519'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233519'>臣今月二十八日准尚书省劄子，奉圣旨，除臣参知政事，日下供职者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233519_comment'></div>臣闻：天下多事，则圣哲驰骛而不足；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233519_comment'></div>天下无事，则庸夫高枕而有馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233519_comment'></div>比自中原震荡以来，天下可谓多事矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233519_comment'></div>陛下焦劳求济，八年于兹，更用大臣，无论数十，终未能仰副圣心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233519_comment'></div>迄至于今，国势未振，陛下当宁慨然，念治愈切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233519_comment'></div>宜于是时得瑰玮卓绝之才，以陪辅帷幄，则戡定祸乱，容或有期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233519_comment'></div>如臣庸愚，一无可纪，躐寘华近，日负尸素之惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233519_comment'></div>今日忽蒙恩除，擢参大政，惊惧陨越，不知所为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233519_comment'></div>傥或冒宠贪荣，不自上列，颠隮累国，所系非轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233519_comment'></div>伏望圣慈特回渊虑，博求人望，改以命之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233519_comment'></div>庶几策虑设施，必能宏济艰难，以克称陛下知人之明，非独臣之幸，实天下幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233519_comment'></div>臣冒渎宸严，无任惶惧战灼之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1233519_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1233519_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年9月</a>　上谢表。作品：《谢除参知政事表》<div id='poem_1233486' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233486' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233486?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢除参知政事表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233486")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233486_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233486'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233486'>召还朝著，久怀未报之恩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233486_comment'></div>擢与政涂，忽拜已成之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233486_comment'></div>顾丹悰之屡控，念渊听之莫回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233486_comment'></div>宠极而忧，感深以惧<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233486_comment'></div>伏念臣起家农圃，托业诗书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233486_comment'></div>寖惊麋鹿之姿，进躐鹓鸾之序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233486_comment'></div>落落难合，恃直道而靡它；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233486_comment'></div>皓皓易污，抚危踪而甚慄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233486_comment'></div>每闻九重尝胆之誓，妄发一介婴鳞之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233486_comment'></div>见谓小忠，曲蒙殊奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233486_comment'></div>虽中外之使令莫效，而初终之眷遇不衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233486_comment'></div>欲竭微劳，敢遗馀力？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233486_comment'></div>讵意圣神之求旧，遽先髦畯而用臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1233486_comment'></div>骤寘庙堂，参陪帷幄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1233486_comment'></div>况四郊多垒之际，赞一日万几之繁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1233486_comment'></div>蒐粟练兵，适欲靖方隅之乱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1233486_comment'></div>图事揆策，又将振朝廷之威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1233486_comment'></div>孰谓薄才，能胜重任？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1233486_comment'></div>莫遂循墙之请，更胜据蒺之思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1233486_comment'></div>勉奉温言，实形惭汗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1233486_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下恢张庶政，延揽群才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1233486_comment'></div>怜臣孤立于时，素受腹心之托；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1233486_comment'></div>察臣多阅于事，庸备股肱之求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1233486_comment'></div>亟下异除，悉从英断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1233486_comment'></div>臣敢不依附日月，警戒夙宵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1233486_comment'></div>同寅协恭，深惩比德之害；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1233486_comment'></div>砥名砺节，上副康功之图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1233486_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1233486_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年10月1日</a>　十月初一，在临安，力赞高宗亲征。高宗赐御书《车攻》诗，上谢表。作品：《谢赐御书车攻诗表》<div id='poem_1233491' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233491' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233491?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢赐御书车攻诗表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年10月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233491")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233491_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233491'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233491'>使镳驰骛，俯传天语之温；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233491_comment'></div>宸翰骞腾，上应奎文之烂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233491_comment'></div>光生箧笥，荣动搢绅<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233491_comment'></div>伏念臣猥以凡才，叨蒙异奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233491_comment'></div>每奉万几之暇，数窥一札之工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233491_comment'></div>至若采石鼓之遗篇，洒银钩之妙迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233491_comment'></div>因辞见意，更踰宵雅之肄三；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233491_comment'></div>与世作程，弥识帝书之第一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233491_comment'></div>敢图珍赐，遽及孤生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233491_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下盛德日新，多能天纵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233491_comment'></div>将芟夷于大难，以绍开于中兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233491_comment'></div>悯周室之诗亡，四夷未靖；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233491_comment'></div>笑宋武之字大，八法不传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1233491_comment'></div>故于游戏笔墨之间，不忘恢复境土之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1233491_comment'></div>怜臣衰钝，贲此宠休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1233491_comment'></div>臣谨当袭藏私门，传宝来裔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1233491_comment'></div>泛洪源而俟舟楫，远符遇主之荣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1233491_comment'></div>因田猎而选车徒，庶裨复古之政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1233491_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1233491_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年10月</a>　上谢恩札子。作品：《谢赐御书车攻诗札子》<div id='poem_1233527' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233527' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233527?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢赐御书车攻诗劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233527")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233527_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233527'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233527'>臣近蒙圣恩，赐臣御书《车攻》诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233527_comment'></div>今又蒙陛下以臣草芥贱名，特纡宸翰，俾获刻于《车攻》篇末，托于不朽，奎钩烂然，光动心目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233527_comment'></div>臣之荣幸，殆绝一时，自顾么微，岂能称塞？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233527_comment'></div>拜赐之际，感涕交颐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233527_comment'></div>仰惟陛下方修复古之政，以图攘狄之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233527_comment'></div>而臣猥以空疏，待罪近列，策虑无取，宜在谴诃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233527_comment'></div>拜此殊私，以惭以惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233527_comment'></div>惟是毕命夙宵，以赞中兴之业，则臣之志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233527_comment'></div>何敢言报？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233527_comment'></div>臣无任感天荷圣激切屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233527_comment'></div>谨具劄子奏谢以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233527_comment'></div>谨奏。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1233527_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年10月4日</a>　十月初四，在临安。赞高宗捐内帑以充岁币。又赞高宗善御将。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年10月8日</a>　十月初八，在临安，奏刘洪道知明州罪状。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年10月9日</a>　十月初九，在临安。奏罢所赐己衣带鞍马。上辞免札子。作品：《辞免赐金带札子》<div id='poem_1233520' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233520' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233520?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免赐金带劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年10月9日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233520")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233520_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233520'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233520'>臣今月初七日正谢，伏蒙圣恩，例赐臣对衣、金带、鱼袋、鞍马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233520_comment'></div>缘臣于初六日已蒙圣恩特降中使赐臣毬纹笏、头带、鱼袋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233520_comment'></div>今来傥或更拜匪颁之式，则是叠冒宠私，在臣愚分，不遑安处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233520_comment'></div>伏望睿慈将例赐金带、鱼袋特行寝罢，庶遵彝典，免致烦言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233520_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1233520_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年10月11日</a>　十月十一日，在临安，论战前遣使故事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年10月13日</a>　十月十三日，在临安。因胡松年往江上与诸将议进兵事，以参知政事兼权枢密院事。劝高宗戒韩世忠作战持重。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年10月21日</a>　十月二十一日，在临安，奏金人和议之策不足信。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年10月22日</a>　十月二十二日，在临安。以敌骑往来于淮甸，奏请高宗遣岳飞自上流乘虚击之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年10月23日</a>　十月二十三日，离临安，扈从高宗亲征。同日，至临平镇。与高宗论对诸将赏罚宜公。草诏书。作品：《亲征戒谕州县诏》<div id='poem_1233432' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233432' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233432?labeling=true' target='_blank'>亲征戒谕州县诏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴四年十月二十三日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年10月23日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233432")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233432_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233432'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233432'>朕以逆臣刘豫称兵南向，警奏既闻，神人共愤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233432_comment'></div>朕不敢复蹈往辙，为退避自安之计，而重贻江浙赤子流离屠戮之祸，乃下罪己诏，亲总六师，临幸江滨，督励将士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233432_comment'></div>然兴师十万，日费千金，动众劳人，惧所不免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233432_comment'></div>每一念此，恻然疚怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233432_comment'></div>尚觊监司帅守与夫郡邑小大之臣夙夜究心，体朕此意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233432_comment'></div>凡借贷催科有须于众者，毋或纵吏并缘为奸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233432_comment'></div>凡盗贼奸宄辄生窥伺者，务绝其萌，毋令窃发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233432_comment'></div>其或乘时抢攘，恣无名之敛，容奸玩寇，失几察之方，至使吾民横罹困苦，有一于此，必罚无赦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233432_comment'></div>候军事稍平，当遣廷臣循行郡国。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1233432_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233489?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免扈从转官表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年2月8日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233489'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233489'>褒典超踰，敢倾危悃；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233489_comment'></div>宠辞敦勉，尚啬俞音<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233489_comment'></div>伏念臣猥以薄材，误蒙殊用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233489_comment'></div>属羽书之纷奏，扈革辂以亲征。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233489_comment'></div>协赞宸谟，既乏徙薪之策；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233489_comment'></div>肃清边警，又无横草之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233489_comment'></div>躐进崇阶，坐饕异赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233489_comment'></div>虽圣恩之过厚，在愚分以难安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233489_comment'></div>忝冒何名，人言必至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233489_comment'></div>控陈未力，天听莫回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233489_comment'></div>再犯雷霆之威，更殚蝼蚁之恳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233489_comment'></div>伏望皇帝陛下推仁从欲，体道观能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233489_comment'></div>念帷幄之近联，已为荣耀；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1233489_comment'></div>收丝纶之成命，庶免颠隮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1233489_comment'></div>倘私愿之获伸，亦公器之增重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1233489_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1233489_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年2月</a>　上谢表。作品：《谢扈从转官表》<div id='poem_1233490' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233490' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233490?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢扈从转官表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233490")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233490_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233490'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233490'>灵旗电扫，克成却敌之功；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233490_comment'></div>清跸天旋，奚举畴劳之典。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233490_comment'></div>固辞弗获，冒受奚堪<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233490_comment'></div>窃以逆臣逋诛，久宽鈇钺；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233490_comment'></div>黠虏借助，复动干戈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233490_comment'></div>边遽初闻，宸谟已决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233490_comment'></div>乘六师之共愤，屈万乘以亲征。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233490_comment'></div>貔貅鼓行，蛇豕奔北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233490_comment'></div>既献俘而奏凯，宜告庙而策勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233490_comment'></div>臣于其间，一无所补，猥缘近列，滥进崇阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233490_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下比迹尧仁，同符汤勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233490_comment'></div>威加敌国，更收不杀之恩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233490_comment'></div>礼厚臣邻，宁畀无名之赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1233490_comment'></div>倘因徽数，用劝群工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1233490_comment'></div>而臣选懦弗强，迂疏何取？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1233490_comment'></div>修车攻复古之政，虽许与闻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1233490_comment'></div>从奉天定难之臣，则为忝窃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1233490_comment'></div>尚图微效，庶答鸿私。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1233490_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年2月13日</a>　二月十三日，在临安，草诏书。作品：《亲征诏》<div id='poem_1233430' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233430' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233430?labeling=true' target='_blank'>亲征诏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴五年二月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年2月13日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233430")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233430_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233430'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233430'>朕猥以寡昧，属兹艰虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233430_comment'></div>迫臣民爱戴之诚，续正统于将坠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233430_comment'></div>痛父兄播迁之难，履尊位以何安？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233430_comment'></div>夙夜以图，策虑并用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233430_comment'></div>岂不能躬擐甲胄，亲冒烟尘，乘将士欲战之心，慰黎元厌乱之意？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233430_comment'></div>然以两宫万里，一别九年，觊迎銮辂之还，期遂庭闱之奉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233430_comment'></div>故暴虎冯河之怒，敌虽逞于凶残；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233430_comment'></div>而投鼠忌器之嫌，朕宁甘于屈辱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233430_comment'></div>是以卑辞厚币，遣使通和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233430_comment'></div>庶殚孝悌之思，必徇哀恫之请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233430_comment'></div>至于土地梗绝，生齿流离。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233430_comment'></div>师徒怀暴露之忧，闾里起绎骚之叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233430_comment'></div>繇朕不德，嗟彼何辜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1233430_comment'></div>仰怀故国之庙祧，至于霣涕；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1233430_comment'></div>俯见中原之父老，宁不汗颜？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1233430_comment'></div>比得敌疆之情，稍有休兵之议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1233430_comment'></div>而叛臣刘豫惧祸及身，造为事端，间谍和好，信逆雏之狂悖，率群偷而陆梁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1233430_comment'></div>借彼援师，倚为威势；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1233430_comment'></div>签我赤子，胁使征行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1233430_comment'></div>涉地称兵，操戈犯顺，大逆不道，一至于斯！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1233430_comment'></div>警奏既闻，神人共愤，猛士在列，怒发上冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1233430_comment'></div>以谓逆顺之理既分，胜负之形可见，皆愿挺身而效死，不忍与贼而俱生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1233430_comment'></div>朕乃下诏总师，卜日引道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1233430_comment'></div>前驱方戒，积阴顿开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1233430_comment'></div>天地鬼神罔不助顺，将帅辅弼罔不协心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1233430_comment'></div>今朕此行，士气百倍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1233430_comment'></div>虽自纂承之后，每乖举措之方，尚念祖宗在天之灵，共刷国家累岁之耻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1233430_comment'></div>殪彼逆党，成此隽功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1233430_comment'></div>载惟风霜跋履之勤，仍蹈锋镝战争之苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1233430_comment'></div>兴言及此，无所措躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1233430_comment'></div>然而能建非常之功，必有不次之赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1233430_comment'></div>初诏具在，朕不食言。</div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1233430_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年2月23日</a>　二月二十三日，在临安。以措置防秋功，转一官，除大中大夫。上辞免札子。作品：《辞免转官札子》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年闰2月3日</a>　闰二月初三，在临安。因胡松年引疾去职，以参知政事再兼权枢密院事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年闰2月8日</a>　闰二月初八，在临安，奏行神主朝谒之礼。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年闰2月11日</a>　闰二月十一日，在临安，与孟庾并兼权枢密院事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年闰2月23日</a>　闰二月二十三日，在临安，奏郡守遴选事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年闰2月26日</a>　闰二月二十六日，在临安，论选官宜重法家之选。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年4月5日</a>　四月初五，在临安，草诏书。作品：《赐韩世忠诏》<div id='poem_1233435' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233435' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233435?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐韩世忠诏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴五年四月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年4月5日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233435")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233435_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233435'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233435'>览奏，欲依旧留屯淮甸，誓与敌人决于一战，已悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233435_comment'></div>朕迫于强敌，越在海隅，每慨然有恢复中原之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233435_comment'></div>顾以频年事力未振，姑郁郁于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233435_comment'></div>自去冬敌人深入，卿首挫其锋，鼓我六师，人百其勇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233435_comment'></div>既至，潜师引遁，而卿复率先移屯淮甸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233435_comment'></div>进取之计，恃此为基，朕甚嘉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233435_comment'></div>前日恐老小或有未便，委卿相度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233435_comment'></div>今得所奏，益见忠诚，虽古名将，殆无以过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233435_comment'></div>使朕竦然兴叹，以谓有臣如此，祸难不足平也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233435_comment'></div>古人有言：「阃外之事，将军制之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233435_comment'></div>今既营屯安便，控制得宜，卿可施置自便，勿复拘执。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233435_comment'></div>至于军饷等事，已令三省施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233435_comment'></div>方此酷暑，将士良劳，行饬使人赍赐夏药抚问，卿并宜知之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1233435_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年4月7日</a>　四月初七，在临安。与赵鼎共赞高宗亲书《无逸》等图置于讲壁。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年4月16日</a>　四月十六日，在临安。赞高宗忧民、不忘祖宗创业之艰。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年5月24日</a>　五月二十四日，在临安，与张浚同提举详定一司。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年6月12日</a>　六月十二日，在临安。因天久旱，与赵鼎、孟庾等奏请革职待罪。上乞罢政札子。作品：《与左相等为亢旱乞罢政札子》<div id='poem_1233523' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233523' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233523?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与左相等为亢旱乞罢政劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴五年六月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年6月12日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233523")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233523_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233523'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233523'>臣等伏见天示变异，亢阳为灾，乃五月丙子不雨，迄至于今，越四旬矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233523_comment'></div>在田之稼，将欲就槁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233523_comment'></div>中心惴慄，恐害有秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233523_comment'></div>伏惟陛下畏天之威，责躬引咎，精意祷祈，无所不至，而星象昭回，甘泽未应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233523_comment'></div>良由臣等叨冒近司，辅政无状，致斯谴告，仰贻圣忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233523_comment'></div>伏望陛下特降威命，正臣等之罪，早赐黜责，庶几上答天心，召来和气，以副云霓之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233523_comment'></div>臣等无任激切之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233523_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1233523_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年6月</a>　再上乞罢政札子。作品：《再与左相等为亢旱乞罢政札子》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年6月</a>　是月，在临安，草诏书。作品：《赐岳飞诏》<div id='poem_1233441' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233441' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233441?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐岳飞诏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴五年六月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233441")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233441_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233441'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233441'>比得张浚奏，知湖湘之寇悉已肃清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233441_comment'></div>纾朕顾忧，良用欣惬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233441_comment'></div>非卿威名冠世，忠略济时，先声所临，人自信服，则何以平积年啸聚之党于旬朝指顾之间？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233441_comment'></div>不烦诛夷，坐获嘉靖，使朕恩威兼畅，厥功茂焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233441_comment'></div>腹心之患既除，进取之图可议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233441_comment'></div>缅思规画，嘉叹不忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233441_comment'></div>然恐招抚之初，人怀反侧，更宜绥辑，以安众情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233441_comment'></div>措置得宜，彼自驯扰，必与卿计之熟矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233441_comment'></div>或有陈请，可具奏来。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1233441_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年7月8日</a>　七月初八，在临安。以孟庾罢，兼权枢密院事及措置财用。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年7月22日</a>　七月二十二日，在临安。奏恤民耕田事宜。同日，因刘商霖上书控告迪功郎沈宇，并指宇为与求族人，家居待罪。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年7月23日</a>　七月二十三日，在临安。得释。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年7月26日</a>　七月二十六日，在临安，有文。作品：《水陆报应记》<div id='poem_1233670' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233670' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233670?labeling=true' target='_blank'>水陆报应记<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴五年七月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年7月26日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233670")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233670_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233670'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233670'>赵丞相云：顷年关中闻有一士人被酒，夜卧于道傍堆阜之上，梦有人呼曰：「城南某人家设水陆，我辈当乘此托生，可同往」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233670_comment'></div>堆阜之下有人叹曰：「一醉人卧于吾上，出不得，奈何」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233670_comment'></div>未几，前所呼者复至，曰：「水陆甚盛，但不甚精洁，圣贤不降，不为利益」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233670_comment'></div>若有嘘嗟之声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233670_comment'></div>已而曰：「久饥，粗得一饱」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233670_comment'></div>其人复应曰：「饥甚，虽一饱亦不可得，是无福也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233670_comment'></div>旦而视之，堆阜乃一古冢也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233670_comment'></div>鬼神之事茫昧难知，然水陆报应甚多，大抵不可不精洁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233670_comment'></div>今因儿子往妙香营设此供，故录示长老佛智大师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233670_comment'></div>绍兴五年七月丁酉必先书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1233670_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年9月5日</a>　九月初五，在临安。论取进士避官人、擢寒士故事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年9月12日</a>　九月十二日，在临安。与赵鼎共赞高宗英断，使士兵精强。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年10月</a>　十月，在临安，草诏书。作品：《赐李纲诏》《赐吕颐浩诏》<div id='poem_1233445' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233445' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233445?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐吕颐浩诏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴五年十月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233445")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233445_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233445'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233445'>朕以湖湘八州之地西通巴蜀，为国上游，往连盗区，一方骚动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233445_comment'></div>比者招辑虽已略平，而民俗剽轻，或易生变，允藉耆德往填抚之，乃起卿燕閒之中，而属以方面之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233445_comment'></div>庶期谈笑坐以销萌，慰彼黎元，增重形势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233445_comment'></div>而抗章固避，殊咈于怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233445_comment'></div>惟卿社稷元老，身任安危，必不以内外为间，谅应闻命，慨然引途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233445_comment'></div>故兹亲笔诏谕，卿宜悉之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1233445_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年</a>　是年，在临安，拟御试策题。作品：《拟御试策题》<div id='poem_1233454' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233454' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233454?labeling=true' target='_blank'>拟御试策题</a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233454")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233454_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233454'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233454'>朕德菲陋，绍承大统。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233454_comment'></div>遭家多难，求济未获。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233454_comment'></div>是以博延豪俊，咸造在庭，觊闻治道之要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233454_comment'></div>子大夫其必尽精极虑，乐为朕言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233454_comment'></div>盖闻在昔圣王之治天下，正心诚意躬行乎上者，固自有道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233454_comment'></div>而措诸事业之间，则或宽或猛，或质或文，变通随时，不胶于迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233454_comment'></div>故其成效布在方册，昭昭乎其可观也，朕甚慕之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233454_comment'></div>越自即位，九年于此矣，愚欲雪父兄之耻，而复祖宗之烈，夙夜祗惧，罔敢荒宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233454_comment'></div>而施为缪盭，治效缺然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233454_comment'></div>深惟其故，不惮改作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233454_comment'></div>间者乃下铨量之令以择吏，而真才犹未显也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233454_comment'></div>严科歛之禁以恤民，而实惠犹未孚也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233454_comment'></div>谨简练之法以治兵，而冗食犹未革也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1233454_comment'></div>夫吏道未肃，民力未苏，兵势未强，朕之治所以未效也，顾何以辑事功、弭祸乱哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1233454_comment'></div>而建议之臣并欲考课以核殿最，省官以抑奉稍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1233454_comment'></div>力役不足以供饷馈也，为之屯戍营田以宽之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1233454_comment'></div>赋入不足以给调度也，为之平准均输以佐之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1233454_comment'></div>爵赏未艾也，为之定武功之等；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1233454_comment'></div>纪律未明也，为之参府卫之制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1233454_comment'></div>凡若此者，其合于古、便于今乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1233454_comment'></div>其或有不然者邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1233454_comment'></div>虽然，此治之迹也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1233454_comment'></div>上之欲三辰明，四时序，灾沴不生而动植遂性；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1233454_comment'></div>下之欲风化行，习俗厚，奸宄不作而中外协心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1233454_comment'></div>兹可以占天人之助矣，夫何敌不克，何难不济？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1233454_comment'></div>兴复大业，其庶几乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1233454_comment'></div>子大夫以为何修何营而可以臻此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1233454_comment'></div>其条列而茂明之，务适于用，朕将有稽焉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1233454_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年1月18日</a>　正月，在临安。十八日，以在政不与闻大事，乞罢去。上乞出札子。作品：《乞出札子》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年</a>　再上乞出札子。作品：《乞出第二札子》<div id='poem_1233529' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233529' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233529?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞出第二劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233529")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233529_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233529'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233529'>臣今早曾具劄子，以臣智愚昏逾，不足谋国，遂沥恳诚，仰干天听，乞一在外宫观差遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233529_comment'></div>伏蒙圣慈特颁宸翰，批降处分，丁宁委曲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233529_comment'></div>仰惟天地父母之恩至深至厚，非臣糜捐所能称塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233529_comment'></div>重念臣猥以一介庸陋之资，遭遇圣明，越先群俊，拔擢至此，曾未有丝发之功以报陛下，何敢数为去就，自干犯上之诛？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233529_comment'></div>顾于朝廷大议多不预闻，此必有以疑臣者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233529_comment'></div>而臣虽有忧国之心，动成嫌间，尸位素餐，每深惭负，彊颜就列，实不遑安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233529_comment'></div>臣见家居待命，未敢随班奏事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233529_comment'></div>伏望圣慈曲垂矜悯，俾臣退就外祠，少养疾病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233529_comment'></div>他日陛下傥赐记怜，则捐躯之期似或未晚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233529_comment'></div>臣无任沥恳祈哀之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233529_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1233529_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年</a>　上乞出札子。作品：《乞出第三札子》《乞出第四札子》《乞出第五札子》《乞出第六札子》《乞出第七札子》《乞出第八札子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（备注：与求于本年正月十八日上第一《乞出札子》，而其于本年二月二十五日罢参知政事，可知其八篇《乞出札子》必作于正月十八日与二月二十五日之间。）</span><div id='poem_1233530' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233530' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233530?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞出第三劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233530")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233530_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233530'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233530'>臣比尝两具奏劄，乞一在外宫观差遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233530_comment'></div>伏蒙圣慈宣谕丁宁，仰荷恩私，不胜感涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233530_comment'></div>然臣有区区之愚，不免干犯斧钺，再控危诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233530_comment'></div>重念臣智术空疏，材力绵弱，叨侍帷幄，无所裨补，夙夜震惧，不遑安息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233530_comment'></div>岂不知同力一心，共赞恢复，必不以进取为非，第欲审而后动耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233530_comment'></div>而臣前日初不闻其曲折，遂有奏陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233530_comment'></div>若诚即有所为，则是臣暗于事机，谋议牴牾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233530_comment'></div>若犹未也，则是臣实失于轻信，致有忧疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233530_comment'></div>况二相之外，惟臣参预机务，有大举措，每以不知其详而忧疑牴牾，岂可复陪国论？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233530_comment'></div>伏望天慈特加矜悯，俾臣解罢机务，退就外祠，少养疾病，尚图他日必有捐躯之所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233530_comment'></div>臣无任恳祈迫切之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233530_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1233530_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1233532' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233532' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233532?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞出第四劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233532")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233532_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233532'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233532'>臣昨以庸陋，误被圣知，越先英豪，擢寘近列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233532_comment'></div>适当前岁，虏犯淮壖，扈跸总师，前临大敌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233532_comment'></div>荷陛下眷遇之深，凡帷幄密议，皆获纤悉与闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233532_comment'></div>臣亦思所奋励，图报万一，而愚虑无补，夙夜不敢自安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233532_comment'></div>及虏骑遁逃之后，事归督府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233532_comment'></div>凡有谋议，虽胥吏辈往往皆知，而臣职在参陪国论，每独不知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233532_comment'></div>臣以此益自愧惧，累尝沥恳丐閒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233532_comment'></div>陛下眷留，未容臣去，辄复奏陈恢复大略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233532_comment'></div>区区愚忠，本图协济，不谓张浚过有嫌疑，动辄相外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233532_comment'></div>前日浚仓遽而来，人情惊詾，以谓相臣动静，必不苟然，奔赴阙庭，当有大议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233532_comment'></div>臣既未以罪去，理合商量，委曲询之，藐不告语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233532_comment'></div>及臣留身具奏，曲折方闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233532_comment'></div>玉音宣谕：今日措置，略如卿初言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1233532_comment'></div>臣仰蒙陛下待以腹心，终始如一，圣恩深厚，感极涕零，岂不怀恋轩墀，誓殚犬马之力？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1233532_comment'></div>然今事之举动，系国安危，而臣乃不得与闻，自古未有此比，岂敢含糊在列？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1233532_comment'></div>欲望圣慈特赐矜悯，除臣一在外宫观差遣，以安愚分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1233532_comment'></div>臣无任沥恳祈哀之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1233532_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1233532_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1233533' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233533' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233533?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞出第五劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233533")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233533_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233533'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233533'>臣以前日相臣仓遽而来，中外惊詾，以谓奔诣阙庭，必有非常之议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233533_comment'></div>而臣叨侍帷幄，又复不获与闻，夙夜怀惭，俯仰跼蹐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233533_comment'></div>遂披诚悃，上渎宸聪，乞解繁机，退安散地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233533_comment'></div>伏蒙圣慈特降中使宣押随班奏事，及赴都堂治事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233533_comment'></div>仰荷圣恩，曲全体貌，虽臣糜殒，岂足报偿？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233533_comment'></div>再念臣自被亲除，至参大政，数陈恢复之略，本有协济之心，而臣才力弗彊，智数无取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233533_comment'></div>惟主知之独厚，顾宰论之莫闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233533_comment'></div>服在股肱，愧形面目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233533_comment'></div>虽艰难之际，敢怀静退以安身？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233533_comment'></div>然几微之閒，恐以猜嫌而累国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233533_comment'></div>不免再殚危恳，冒犯天威，欲望特赐矜怜，检会臣前奏，除一在外宫观差遣，庶全孤节，尚励后图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233533_comment'></div>臣无任祈天望圣激切屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233533_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1233533_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1233534' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233534' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233534?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞出第六劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233534")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233534_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233534'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233534'>臣比者荐输危悃，冒犯宸严，乞解政机，除一在外宫观差遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233534_comment'></div>伏蒙圣慈再降中使，宣押赴都堂治事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233534_comment'></div>恩眷优渥，不替初终，报效莫从，唯知陨涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233534_comment'></div>伏念臣顷繇孤远，遭遇圣明，感于知怜，思所奋励。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233534_comment'></div>常谓议和避地，恐成微弱之形；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233534_comment'></div>积粟练兵，审图恢拓之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233534_comment'></div>念刍言之曲折，荷天语之褒嘉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233534_comment'></div>志在必成，期于协济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233534_comment'></div>而臣终缘拙直，动致忌嫌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233534_comment'></div>适偶相臣奔赴行阙，惟是人情詾惧之际，莫闻国论安危之几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233534_comment'></div>名曰参陪，实均责任，疏外若此，尸素何安？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233534_comment'></div>惟恃保全之恩，未至颠隮之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233534_comment'></div>俯仰循省，夙夜惊惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1233534_comment'></div>是以不避渎烦，备陈覼缕，仰祈睿听，曲赐矜怜，授以宫祠，投之散地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1233534_comment'></div>庶欲全于国体，岂敢恤于身谋？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1233534_comment'></div>拳拳愚忠，莫尽于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1233534_comment'></div>臣无任祈天望圣激切屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1233534_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1233534_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1233535' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233535' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233535?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞出第七劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233535")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233535_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233535'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233535'>臣比沥血诚，冒尘天听，乞解机务，退就祠宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233535_comment'></div>伏蒙圣恩，曲全体貌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233535_comment'></div>使华宣押，于再于三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233535_comment'></div>待遇优隆，始终如一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233535_comment'></div>感深沦骨，涕泪交流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233535_comment'></div>伏念臣立身奇孤，赋性惷直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233535_comment'></div>仰恃主眷，自信不疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233535_comment'></div>而臣识虑不足以察人情之微，谋谟不足以陪国论之末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233535_comment'></div>数陈恢复之略，本有协济之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233535_comment'></div>嫌间既萌，龃龉难合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233535_comment'></div>惟是乞身而去，兹乃昔贤之规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233535_comment'></div>伏望睿慈特赐矜悯，亟从私欲，免累误知，则臣未死之年，皆是捐躯之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233535_comment'></div>臣无任祈天望圣激切屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1233535_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1233535_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1233536' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233536' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233536?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞出第八劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233536")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233536_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233536'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233536'>臣伏蒙圣恩，以臣乞解机务，退就祠宫，赐臣诏书不允者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233536_comment'></div>需奏渎烦，累陈危悃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233536_comment'></div>玺书慰勉，尚啬俞音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233536_comment'></div>伏读训词，惟知感涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233536_comment'></div>窃念臣以一介无庸之质，荷万乘非常之知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233536_comment'></div>孤立于朝，自信所学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233536_comment'></div>每欲同寅而许国，第知直道以事君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233536_comment'></div>顾愚忠之不移，宜此身之必去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233536_comment'></div>盍归畎亩，难恋轩墀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233536_comment'></div>弥切拳拳之心，匪萌倖倖之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233536_comment'></div>仰祈睿鉴，曲轸慈怜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233536_comment'></div>终赐保全，亟降处分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233536_comment'></div>庶存去就，不负生成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1233536_comment'></div>臣无任祈天望圣激切屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1233536_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1233536_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年2月12日</a>　二月十二日，在临安，草诏书。作品：《赐川陕宣抚处置司诏》《赐吴玠王彦关师古奖谕勅书》<div id='poem_1233431' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233431' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233431?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐川陕宣抚处置使司诏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴六年二月十二日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年2月12日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233431")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233431_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233431'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233431'>朕绍国丕基，遭时多难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233431_comment'></div>饬戎车于江左，为怀经略之图；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233431_comment'></div>列将钺于关中，欲存根本之势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233431_comment'></div>岂虞强国，专逞淫威。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233431_comment'></div>敌劲弗支，兵拿未解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233431_comment'></div>嗟苍天之不吊，宜悔祸于我家；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233431_comment'></div>悯赤子之无辜，重流毒于兹土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233431_comment'></div>寡德所致，悼心何言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233431_comment'></div>赖我股肱之臣，总护爪牙之任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233431_comment'></div>一战克捷，群丑歼夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233431_comment'></div>王灵由是复加，士气于焉再振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233431_comment'></div>然念兴师累岁，转斗一方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233431_comment'></div>被夷狄之系累，宁无沦陷之党；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1233431_comment'></div>思祖宗之涵养，岂有背叛之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1233431_comment'></div>凭陵使然，蹭蹬至此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1233431_comment'></div>傥存疑阻，殊咈招徕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1233431_comment'></div>将束身而欲归，或惧刑诛之惨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1233431_comment'></div>比复业而奠处，或忧赋役之烦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1233431_comment'></div>或立效而褒赏未加，或负才而禄秩未称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1233431_comment'></div>疾苦无告，愁恨何聊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1233431_comment'></div>仄席以思，当馈而叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1233431_comment'></div>于是下哀痛之诏，布至意以宣昭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1233431_comment'></div>施旷荡之恩，洗庶辜而抆拭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1233431_comment'></div>沿边将士应陷蕃之人，非抗王师及侵掠入寇者，并不得诛杀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1233431_comment'></div>虏骑冯陵之际，陷没州县官吏将士军民，皆缘事力不能捍御，致有胁从，或遭驱虏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1233431_comment'></div>至今困居本土，或旅寓远边，实为残破，无曰背叛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1233431_comment'></div>陷蕃之人能立功来归者，仰沿边帅守保举，申宣抚司一面旌擢优赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1233431_comment'></div>其次虽未能立功，而心在本朝，有意怀来者，各以元旧官职任使；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1233431_comment'></div>兵级弓箭手依旧职名收管，民兵愿归业者听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1233431_comment'></div>其间才力可用，特与拔擢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1233431_comment'></div>或有以前罪犯，怀疑自危，一切原贷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1233431_comment'></div>或先曾立功，未曾推赏，即特与推赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1233431_comment'></div>因陷蕃废业失所者，宽其租赋，免其征役。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1233431_comment'></div>昨缘道路不通，号令壅隔，致远方之民疾苦无所赴诉，专委宣抚司讲究措置，并从宽恤，遍下诸处官司施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1233431_comment'></div>咨尔有众，咸识朕心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1233431_comment'></div>各坚奋励之诚，亟臻休息之效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1233431_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_36_1233431_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1233449' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233449' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233449?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐吴玠王彦关师古奖谕敕书<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴元年二月十二日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年2月12日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233449")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233449_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233449'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233449'>朕乘历运之中微，属方隅之多故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233449_comment'></div>兵尘数起，边候屡惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233449_comment'></div>永怀秦雍之区，久罹夷狄之祸，暴骨满野，连城为墟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233449_comment'></div>兴言霣心，引望流涕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233449_comment'></div>式资骁锐之将，屏此腥膻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233449_comment'></div>庶使创残之民，脱于涂炭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233449_comment'></div>卿世家陇右，气禀山西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233449_comment'></div>摅忠愤于胸中，燀威棱于塞外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233449_comment'></div>运奇合变，并施九拒之谋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233449_comment'></div>鼓勇争先，悉用万全之略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233449_comment'></div>潜军一举，迸骑四驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233449_comment'></div>折虏势于方骄，激士心而复振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233449_comment'></div>兹为社稷之卫，良慰鼓鼙之思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1233449_comment'></div>然念岁月倭迟，风霜匽薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1233449_comment'></div>勤勚虽由于尔力，咎责实归于朕躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1233449_comment'></div>更奋鹰扬之师，益歼蚁附之众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1233449_comment'></div>剋复疆土，抚定黎氓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1233449_comment'></div>赤囊之捷系传，功既存于庙祏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1233449_comment'></div>丹书之誓永固，福自及于子孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1233449_comment'></div>各坚乃诚，勿忘朕训。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1233449_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年2月25日</a>　二月二十五日，在临安。罢参知政事，除资政殿学士、知明州。上辞免札子。作品：《辞免资政殿学士知明州札子》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年2月</a>　再上辞免札子。作品：《辞免资政殿学士知明州第二札子》<div id='poem_1233538' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233538' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233538?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免除资政殿学士知明州第二劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233538")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233538_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233538'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233538'>臣猥以一介无能之质，误被圣知，擢陪政路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233538_comment'></div>叨冒无补，夙夜怀惭，遂沥血诚，仰干天听，乞解机务，退就祠宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233538_comment'></div>伏蒙矜怜，曲全体貌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233538_comment'></div>名城峻职，并冒恩荣，岂臣糜捐，所能称塞？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233538_comment'></div>感涕横溢，九殒难酬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233538_comment'></div>臣虽已具恳辞，未奉处分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233538_comment'></div>重念臣朴拙之性，第尽愚忠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233538_comment'></div>孤危之踪，实恃异眷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233538_comment'></div>傥忘素分，定致烦言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233538_comment'></div>欲望天慈，终垂悯察，检会臣累奏，除一在外宫观差遣，庶存晚节，期报大恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233538_comment'></div>臣无任祈天望圣激切屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233538_comment'></div>取进止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233538_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1233538'>〔贴黄〕臣于今月二十一日留身奏事，历陈危悃，既蒙恩许其去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1233538_comment'></div>拜辞天陛之际，玉音宣谕：当全体貌，尽礼而行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1233538_comment'></div>仰荷眷遇始终，感深沦骨，所以跼蹐待命，遂至浃旬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1233538_comment'></div>窃恐中外不知，招致物论，重费陛下保全之赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1233538_comment'></div>伏望天慈早降处分，亟遂宫祠之请，庶免颠隮。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1233538_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年2月</a>　上辞免札子。作品：《辞免资政殿学士知明州第三札子》<div id='poem_1233539' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233539' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233539?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免除资政殿学士知明州第三劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233539")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233539_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233539'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233539'>臣伏蒙圣慈，以臣辞免资政殿学士、知明州恩命，特降诏书不允者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233539_comment'></div>危悃渎烦，粗殚万一；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233539_comment'></div>恩言慰谕，殆至再三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233539_comment'></div>荷圣意之周旋，抚危踪而怵惕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233539_comment'></div>伏念臣奋繇寒士，本乏异能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233539_comment'></div>曲被冕旒之知，参陪廊庙之列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233539_comment'></div>一毫何补，百谪是宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233539_comment'></div>然考平日敷奏之言，曷尝不在于恢复；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233539_comment'></div>推老生朴野之学，亦欲共济于艰难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233539_comment'></div>而孤根易摇，薄命难偶，每于曲折之际，倍费保全之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233539_comment'></div>倾输肺肝，控告君父。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233539_comment'></div>忠虽许国，义盍引身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233539_comment'></div>仰蒙日月之明，俯察蝼蚁之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1233539_comment'></div>诏函使骑，眷礼有加；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1233539_comment'></div>峻职名城，宠荣并至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1233539_comment'></div>既逾私分，荐具恳辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1233539_comment'></div>天听未回，欲全终始之遇；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1233539_comment'></div>人言可畏，恐乖去就之方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1233539_comment'></div>伏望圣慈特赐矜悯，悉收还于成命，亟畀付于真祠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1233539_comment'></div>庶几馀生，免累洪造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1233539_comment'></div>臣无任祈天望圣激切屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1233539_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1233539_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年2月</a>　是月，在临安。中书舍人任申先论与求之罪，复乞在外宫观，遂改提举临安府洞霄宫。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年2月</a>　上谢表。作品：《谢除名宫观表》<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
扬州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='0bd3efd52e83499fb33e19174a77fd04_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("0bd3efd52e83499fb33e19174a77fd04");'><span id='0bd3efd52e83499fb33e19174a77fd04_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1128&endYear=1128')">1128年</a>，43岁</div><div id='0bd3efd52e83499fb33e19174a77fd04' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在扬州。因常同荐，改通直郎。会罢太学，除通判明州，改两浙路提举市舶，未赴。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>冬，在扬州，有诗。作品：《戊申初寒偶作》<div id='poem_538693' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_538693' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/538693?labeling=true' target='_blank'>戊申初寒偶作</a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_538693")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_538693_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_538693'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_538693'>去年十月冬犹温，单衣晓出钱塘门。<div id='poem_sentence_0_538693_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_538693'>携孥仅脱饿虎口，更吟楚些招惊魂。<div id='poem_sentence_1_538693_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_538693'>儿女争从乱离苦，咿哑绕膝多语言。<div id='poem_sentence_2_538693_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_538693'>舟行畏涂侵夜泊，孤灯明灭何处村。<div id='poem_sentence_3_538693_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_538693'>萧萧细雨疏苇响，风力渐摇枯柳根。<div id='poem_sentence_4_538693_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_538693'>失声号寒泣龙具，促棹傍险争前奔。<div id='poem_sentence_5_538693_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_538693'>还家依然四壁立，故衾败絮那忍论。<div id='poem_sentence_6_538693_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_538693'>无衣岂暇具裘褐，海图<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>坼裂波涛翻。<div id='poem_sentence_7_538693_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_538693'>天公戏人亦太虐，雪花径尺连上元。<div id='poem_sentence_8_538693_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_538693'>今年十月事羁宦，两脚如旧身大<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作幸）</span>存。<div id='poem_sentence_9_538693_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_538693'>纸窗寂历风竹啸，古木中夜号空园。<div id='poem_sentence_10_538693_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_538693'>旅人不眠毛骨冷，抚事念往多烦冤。<div id='poem_sentence_11_538693_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_538693'>吾侪小人不论数，豺狼满目哀王孙。<div id='poem_sentence_12_538693_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_538693'>似闻易水寒堕指，北望大漠烟云昏。<div id='poem_sentence_13_538693_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_538693'>安得壮士驭八骏，沙虫猿鹤俱腾骞。<div id='poem_sentence_14_538693_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_538693'>归欤莫如中土乐，天子孝友朝廷尊。<div id='poem_sentence_15_538693_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_538693'>坐令铁衣扫虮虱，四海挟纩怀君恩。<div id='poem_sentence_16_538693_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_538693'></div><div id='poem_sentence_17_538693_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_538693'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_7_538693_0'>⑴ 原作国，据四库本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_538693_comment'></div></div><br /></div>
