-----title
南京
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='02a3c37320294361b20fe1e2c2fcd233_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("02a3c37320294361b20fe1e2c2fcd233");'><span id='02a3c37320294361b20fe1e2c2fcd233_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年</a>，44岁</div><div id='02a3c37320294361b20fe1e2c2fcd233' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年6月27日</a>　六月二十七日，在建康。以张守荐，除监察御史。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年9月</a>　九月，在建康。以潘师仲子请，为其母朱夫人作墓志铭。作品：《朱夫人墓志铭》<div id='poem_1233675' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233675' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233675?labeling=true' target='_blank'>朱夫人墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（建炎三年九月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233675")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233675_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233675'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233675'>夫人朱氏，世为湖州安吉人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233675_comment'></div>父绎，太庙斋郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233675_comment'></div>自其曾高以来，号以赀雄于乡，然儒服蝉联，素风甚饬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233675_comment'></div>夫人幼而庄静，整整有家法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233675_comment'></div>父母爱之，为择良配，得同里潘侯师仲归焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233675_comment'></div>夫人之归，逮事其姑，能先意顺适，卒以孝妇称于族党之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233675_comment'></div>事其夫恭谨，如待遇严宾客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233675_comment'></div>娣姒雍穆，怡怡如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233675_comment'></div>潘侯少小喜自振拔，其交游多四方才士大夫，馆谷如归，至倾家不问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233675_comment'></div>丝竹之娱，帷帐豆觞之具，必极精腆，夫人职之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233675_comment'></div>归十年，生三男子：曰芑、曰莘、曰蕡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233675_comment'></div>潘侯卒时，夫人盛年，既终丧，宜改适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233675_comment'></div>夫人闻之恸绝，自誓，弗许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1233675_comment'></div>然二子甫胜衣，其季在襁褓，未能谁何也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1233675_comment'></div>夫人克奉潘氏祀，字其孤，有幽閒淑慎之操。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1233675_comment'></div>三子既稍长知事，夫人一日斥奁中物几所于庭，悲泣不自胜，呼三子侍旁，且诲之曰：「汝父平生时锲意欲立门户，非苟然者，不幸弃诸孤蚤世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1233675_comment'></div>吾哀亡抚存，虽鞠穷不悔，吾心固有处也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1233675_comment'></div>今汝曹齿宜学，其以诗书起家，成汝父志，顾何以籯金为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1233675_comment'></div>其为汝资，勉之哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1233675_comment'></div>三子相持泣，谨诺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1233675_comment'></div>即招聘四方知名士馆之门下，授以儒术如誓云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1233675_comment'></div>三子资秀发，嶷然可喜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1233675_comment'></div>为学务自刻苦，在侪类中崭崭见头角。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1233675_comment'></div>蕡遂一举中乙科，授迪功郎，调高邮军司兵曹事，迎夫人之官下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1233675_comment'></div>会芑及莘由乡荐肄太学，夫人旦暮念之不衰，蕡乃奉安舆西游上都，以娱其意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1233675_comment'></div>既至，而蕡小疾不起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1233675_comment'></div>夫人以客柩归，卜居郡之西闉，曰：「吾不忘故里，顾吾庐，蕡儿时戏剧及其起居寝饭处，历历在眼中，吾不忍视也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1233675_comment'></div>汝曹脱有立，庶几释吾此哀，不然无以吾归」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1233675_comment'></div>二子奉夫人训，相戒，语激昂，益不懈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1233675_comment'></div>客有相过，夫人从屏间窥之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1233675_comment'></div>其人贤，即色喜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1233675_comment'></div>语谍而意嫚，辄禁切不相还往，故所与游多益者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1233675_comment'></div>亡几何，莘亦相次中第，授迪功郎，调衢州西安县尉，归拜夫人于堂下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1233675_comment'></div>夫人疾已侵，摄衣强起一视之，叹曰：「吾嫠居三十年，天卒相吾二子俱成名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1233675_comment'></div>芑故未偶，度其趣操，宜不坠厥家，吾死何憾」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1233675_comment'></div>夫人畴昔嗜内典，因索其书日诵之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1233675_comment'></div>弥月，忽若有得，默然宴坐，瞑目而逝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1233675_comment'></div>其了达死生，虽学佛之徒，自以弗逮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1233675_comment'></div>实建炎戊申十二月十九日也，享年五十有三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1233675_comment'></div>有孙男六人：曰梅、曰楫、曰楹、曰格、曰权、曰相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1233675_comment'></div>孙女三人，皆幼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1233675_comment'></div>越明年九月某日，诸孤奉夫人之丧归葬于邑之东山凤亭之冈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1233675_comment'></div>将葬，诸孤载夫人语，泣请铭于予。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1233675_comment'></div>予谓人为善患不力，诚力，未有无其报者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1233675_comment'></div>夫人志节终始，凛凛乎不可夺，烈丈夫有愧焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1233675_comment'></div>身见二子躐取名第，起为搢绅家，天之相其为善，获报丰矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1233675_comment'></div>钟釜之禄顾不能一朝享之，殆其赋予然耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1233675_comment'></div>兹亦可悲也已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1233675_comment'></div>三子少从予游，且夫人行应铭，义不得辞，乃为之铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_48_1233675'>其殖也丰，而用之冲，不赢其躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1233675_comment'></div>其节也正，而持之定，不陨其姓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1233675_comment'></div>此古烈妇之所难，而夫人能然，得不为贤也邪！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1233675_comment'></div>是宜神者报之，用锡尔祉，迄成厥家，克昌厥嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1233675_comment'></div>鸣凤之冈，乔木苍苍，铭诗孔昭，百世之藏。</div><div id='poem_sentence_52_1233675_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='a5f39e39269a4180965c5f31d00bdd34_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a5f39e39269a4180965c5f31d00bdd34");'><span id='a5f39e39269a4180965c5f31d00bdd34_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年</a>，52岁</div><div id='a5f39e39269a4180965c5f31d00bdd34' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年3月9日</a>　三月初九，从高宗至建康。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年3月16日</a>　三月十六日，在建康。迁知枢密院事。上辞免表。作品：《辞免除知枢密院事表》<div id='poem_1233499' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233499' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233499?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免除知枢密院事表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1137年3月16日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233499")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233499_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233499'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233499'>宠命频仍，已骇闻于朝著；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233499_comment'></div>愚衷激切，遂冒渎于宸聪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233499_comment'></div>载锡温言，尚稽俞旨<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233499_comment'></div>伏念臣寅缘拙直，被遇圣神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233499_comment'></div>识本昧于经纶，言多涉于迂阔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233499_comment'></div>比自召归帷幄，擢赞枢机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233499_comment'></div>执羁靮以从，虽与近臣而在列；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233499_comment'></div>习金革之事，则非平日之所长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233499_comment'></div>深惧充员，驯致旷职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233499_comment'></div>敢谓眷私之渥，骤升等级之崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233499_comment'></div>并阅三迁，甫更两月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233499_comment'></div>盖大恩稠叠，矜遗簪之复收；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233499_comment'></div>而小器满盈，思覆餗之当戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1233499_comment'></div>纵欲励捐躯之节，讵能忘误国之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1233499_comment'></div>承命惊惶，抚心战掉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1233499_comment'></div>是敢控陈草芥之贱恳，干犯斧钺之严诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1233499_comment'></div>伏望皇帝陛下圣度曲全，皇明下烛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1233499_comment'></div>察臣愚陋之质未有报偿，怜臣衰病之身弗克负荷，亟收误奖，博选真贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1233499_comment'></div>傥获就于旧班，庶免贻于大戾。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1233499_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年</a>　上辞免札子。作品：《辞免除知枢密院事札子》<div id='poem_1233549' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233549' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233549?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免除知枢密院事劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1137年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233549")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233549_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233549'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233549'>臣伏蒙圣恩，除臣知枢密院事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233549_comment'></div>闻命之次，跼蹐靡安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233549_comment'></div>伏念臣顷以至愚极陋之质，久污近联，绩效无闻，退安散地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233549_comment'></div>圣恩记录，遽有经筵之召。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233549_comment'></div>扶持疾病，甫及造朝，亟被诏除，进陪右府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233549_comment'></div>而臣已试无状，沥恳再三，天听莫回，俯偻就职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233549_comment'></div>方欲勉竭驽钝，少报万分，而才分所拘，未有尺寸之效，内怀惭惧，背若负芒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233549_comment'></div>忽蒙超迁，莫测所以，惊惶颤汗，无地自容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233549_comment'></div>陛下之恩，遇臣过厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233549_comment'></div>而臣所自揣，素不知兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233549_comment'></div>既无策画，仰赞庙谟，又无事功，下厌人望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233549_comment'></div>冒处机衡之地，已为非分，而居位未几，复此叨逾，历寻前修，未有其比，天下公议，其将谓何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233549_comment'></div>必至颠隮，重累国体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1233549_comment'></div>伏望陛下廓天地之照，察蝼蚁之诚，特轸深慈，追还成命，俾臣仍旧职任，夙夜黾勉，庶几万一或能少副陛下责任之意，而臣之罪戾亦恐得以少宽，不胜幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1233549_comment'></div>谨具劄子陈免以闻，臣无任祈哀俟命迫切屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1233549_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1233549_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年</a>　上谢表。作品：《谢知枢密院事表》<div id='poem_1233500' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233500' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233500?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢知枢密院事表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1137年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233500")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233500_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233500'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233500'>庀官右府，靡容坐席之温；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233500_comment'></div>出綍中宸，遽躐朝班之峻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233500_comment'></div>宠光沓至，感涕交流<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233500_comment'></div>伏念臣性质滞顽，器能浅薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233500_comment'></div>徒缘异奖，更践要涂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233500_comment'></div>直道难行，阅风波之屡变；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233500_comment'></div>大恩未报，悼蒲柳之先衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233500_comment'></div>顾忝冒之非宜，获屏藏之为幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233500_comment'></div>比膺召节，复赞事枢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233500_comment'></div>病骨支离，愈不胜于策励；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233500_comment'></div>圣谋宏远，将焉副于询求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233500_comment'></div>蚤夜以思，进退维谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233500_comment'></div>岂谓历时未几，身命已加。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1233500_comment'></div>初无尺寸可纪之劳，越在二三同列之右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1233500_comment'></div>闻者甚愕，心其独忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1233500_comment'></div>既控避之弗谐，祇惊惭而罔措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1233500_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下尧舜孝弟，禹汤忧勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1233500_comment'></div>至性过人，方尽宅忧之制；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1233500_comment'></div>沈几先物，不忘复古之图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1233500_comment'></div>如臣孱愚，亦在推择。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1233500_comment'></div>臣敢不恪思其职，勉称所蒙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1233500_comment'></div>事君尽忠之心，造次于是；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1233500_comment'></div>为国复雠之计，死生以之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1233500_comment'></div>庶效涓尘，少酬天地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1233500_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1233500_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年</a>　是月，在建康，有与人回启。作品：《回赵相公启》<div id='poem_1233650' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233650' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233650?labeling=true' target='_blank'>回赵相公启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1137年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233650")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233650_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233650'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233650'>比者滥膺诏綍，参执事枢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233650_comment'></div>未遑坐席之安，更躐朝班之峻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233650_comment'></div>宠私沓至，控微恳而弗俞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233650_comment'></div>忧责并加，抚衰踪而靡称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233650_comment'></div>惧形心骨，愧溢面颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233650_comment'></div>伏念某出自寒家，本非远器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233650_comment'></div>干禄之学，曾不足以禔身；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233650_comment'></div>负薪之言，夫岂堪于谋国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233650_comment'></div>顷缘虚奖，驯致彻官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233650_comment'></div>久贻尸素之讥，甫遂归田之幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233650_comment'></div>圣恩未既，遽因簪履以见收；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233650_comment'></div>愚虑已殚，无复丝毫之云补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233650_comment'></div>不图两月，而阅三迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1233650_comment'></div>属当郊垒之多，曷赞帷筹之秘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1233650_comment'></div>深知忝冒，积负兢惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1233650_comment'></div>此盖伏遇某官道合天民，才优人杰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1233650_comment'></div>功高社稷，久登翊于睿谟；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1233650_comment'></div>望重搢绅，专统盟于善类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1233650_comment'></div>夙借吹嘘之力，曲为根柢之容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1233650_comment'></div>遂使衰年，复叨殊用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1233650_comment'></div>崇墉在望，尚稽感臆之陈；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1233650_comment'></div>宝翰流音，亟辱庆缄之贶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1233650_comment'></div>铭藏之至，敷叙莫周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1233650_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1233650_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年</a>　是月，在建康，有回启。作品：《知枢密院回前宰执启》<div id='poem_1233652' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233652' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233652?labeling=true' target='_blank'>知枢密院回前执政启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1137年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233652")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233652_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233652'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233652'>里巷投閒，方少休于疲曳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233652_comment'></div>岩廊图旧，俄复玷于宠休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233652_comment'></div>顾陈力之不能，当试可而乃已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233652_comment'></div>靡容控避，祇负兢惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233652_comment'></div>某窾启寡闻，尪羸多病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233652_comment'></div>昨以耝耰之质，进与庙堂之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233652_comment'></div>过计拳拳，虽有徙薪之虑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233652_comment'></div>空言落落，卒无横草之功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233652_comment'></div>恐孤奉于明恩，期退藏于晚岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233652_comment'></div>不图远外，犹累简求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233652_comment'></div>□惟枢机之臣，职在甲兵之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233652_comment'></div>未之学也，岂能忘尸素之忧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233652_comment'></div>方且图之，何以济艰危之会？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1233652_comment'></div>拊心惕若，承命赧然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1233652_comment'></div>伏惟某官<span class='inlineComment2'>（云云）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1233652_comment'></div>致是迂愚，复兹忝冒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1233652_comment'></div>时哉不可失，固欲勉于著鞭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1233652_comment'></div>老矣无能为，诚恐贻于覆餗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1233652_comment'></div>尚祈告教，少逭谴何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1233652_comment'></div>犹稽柔牍之修，遽辱珍函之贶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1233652_comment'></div>谦光所逮，朽质为荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1233652_comment'></div>愧感交深，控陈难尽。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1233652_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年4月21日</a>　四月二十一日，在建康，与高宗论刘光世、张浚。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年5月23日</a>　五月二十三日，在建康，书册文。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年</a>　是年，在建康，乞改德清“妙严院”为“功德院”。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年6月15日</a>　六月十五日，卒。赠左银青光禄大夫。谥忠敏。九月二十五日，葬于德清县永和乡马鞍山。<br /></div>
-----end

绍兴

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年10月17日</a>　十月十七日，随高宗至越州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年10月28日</a>　十月二十八日，在越州。上疏论执政过失，除尚书兵部员外郎。自劾言不当，不应得迁，高宗行其言。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='b95567f8067f40d19ec10d8ea6bc7780_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b95567f8067f40d19ec10d8ea6bc7780");'><span id='b95567f8067f40d19ec10d8ea6bc7780_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年</a>，45岁</div><div id='b95567f8067f40d19ec10d8ea6bc7780' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年4月12日</a>　四月十二日，扈从高宗至会稽（即越州）。上陈追敌之计，高宗不纳。建议定都建康。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年5月11日</a>　五月十一日，在越州，奏请高宗随宜措置以答天变，又论刘安世军名等事。高宗纳之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年5月17日</a>　五月十七日，在越州，试侍御史。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年</a>　五、六月间，在越州，三上疏劾周望。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年6月3日</a>　六月初三，在越州，劾连南夫、陈机残扰害民。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年6月22日</a>　六月二十二日，在越州。论人才选拔应不拘一格，高宗不纳。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年7月</a>　七月，在越州。因误奏叶份，上疏待罪。劾李捧、张宗颜、陈思恭三人讨贼不利之过。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年8月8日</a>　八月初八，在越州，与黎确、吴表臣共劾季陵逢迎范宗尹意、乞用罪戾之人。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年8月11日</a>　八月十一日，在越州。以论范宗尹，被罢侍御史，除直龙图阁、知台州。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='a9478cc068c248b5870bf1504cf00fbd_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a9478cc068c248b5870bf1504cf00fbd");'><span id='a9478cc068c248b5870bf1504cf00fbd_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年</a>，46岁</div><div id='a9478cc068c248b5870bf1504cf00fbd' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年7月29日</a>　七月二十九日，在越州，陈范宗尹大罪二十。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年8月6日</a>　八月初六，在越州，再除侍御史。与高宗论王安石，认为其罪首在心术不正。同月，又奏张守荐汪伯彦不当。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年9月1日</a>　九月初一，在越州。奏汪伯彦误国，不可复用。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年9月9日</a>　九月初九，在越州。以杨球不经右选而授文资，乞罢杨球归于右选。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年9月27日</a>　九月二十七日，在越州。陈屯田利害，上《古今集议》两卷。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年9月</a>　九月，在越州。以旧法转废，乞用元丰六察旧法。劾朱胜非避事辞难，致九江陷落。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年11月</a>　十一月，在越州。奏辛永宗、辛道宗、富直柔、韩璜等交结成党，又论李永志同为奸利，致军情不安。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年11月23日</a>　十一月二十三日，在越州。论陈杌贪刻，不可复用。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
湖州

id='poem_sentence_1_1233685_comment'></div>我仕不偶，半世迍邅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233685_comment'></div>鞠穷闵凶，奉我周旋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233685_comment'></div>克相内事，见谓为贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233685_comment'></div>比我叨荣，遭时多艰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233685_comment'></div>空闺无人，谁与话言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233685_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233685_comment'></div>弱子稚女，号呼彻天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233685_comment'></div>失此慈母，谁拊谁怜？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233685_comment'></div>顾瞻山林，卜云未安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1233685_comment'></div>今举君棺，稿葬祗园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1233685_comment'></div>牛衣之泣，尚何可论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1233685_comment'></div>长号永诀，失声烦冤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1233685_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉，尚飨！</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1233685_comment'></div></div></div><br id='poem_sentence_1_1233686_comment'></div>窀穸未安，夙夜靡忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233686_comment'></div>爰得吉卜，大壮之阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233686_comment'></div>与我先垄，乔木相望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233686_comment'></div>将举君柩，兹焉永藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233686_comment'></div>引觞告诀，言出涕滂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233686_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉，尚飨！</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1233686_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>是年，在湖州。与綦处厚共荐李元叔为监察御史。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='6606f0d4a58c470b8bba4ab1ad425b80_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6606f0d4a58c470b8bba4ab1ad425b80");'><span id='6606f0d4a58c470b8bba4ab1ad425b80_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1137')">1136-1137年</a>，51-52岁</div><div id='6606f0d4a58c470b8bba4ab1ad425b80' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年3月</a>　是年三月起，居湖州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年9月21日</a>　九月二十一日，在湖州。以《禄秩》成书，诏转一官。上辞免札子。作品：《辞免敕令所修书成转官札子》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年</a>　再上辞免札子。作品：《辞免敕令所修书成转官第二札子》<div id='poem_1233542' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233542' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233542?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免敕令所修书成转官第二劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233542")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233542_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233542'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233542'>臣十月十三日准行在都进奏院递到告一道，以《禄秩新书》成转臣一官；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233542_comment'></div>及奉诏书，以臣辞免上件恩命，未蒙矜允者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233542_comment'></div>天地之恩，固欲从厚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233542_comment'></div>蝼蚁之志，终冀获申。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233542_comment'></div>罔避黩烦，荐形敷叙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233542_comment'></div>窃以上之行赏无滥则人劝，下之被赏无愧则身荣，授受之间，得失所系。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233542_comment'></div>傥事功之未称，顾分义之何安？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233542_comment'></div>贪得不言，冒荣孰甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233542_comment'></div>惟新书定禄秩之等，命近臣兼提督之官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233542_comment'></div>虽用故常，曾蒙委使，而讨论沿革，裒辑散亡，则有司存，在臣何力？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233542_comment'></div>矧复属稿之始，臣已去朝，历时之多，书方奏御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233542_comment'></div>而臣论功无有，受赏何名？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233542_comment'></div>褒典横加，惊惶失措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1233542_comment'></div>是以辄陈奏牍，力具恳辞，俞音未颁，危衷益惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1233542_comment'></div>此虽陛下亲乘戎辂，赫然有为之时，而臣退安祠宫，冒此无功之赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1233542_comment'></div>人诛鬼责，将不赦臣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1233542_comment'></div>公议私情，皆恐累国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1233542_comment'></div>思念朝夕，怵惕冰渊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1233542_comment'></div>伏望宸慈特回天听，察臣愚悃，实非饰辞，矜从既竭之诚，追寝已成之命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1233542_comment'></div>庶于素分，行以少安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1233542_comment'></div>仰望行阙，臣无任恳倒迫切之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1233542_comment'></div>所有告命，臣见寄纳湖州军资库，不敢祗受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1233542_comment'></div>谨再具劄子陈免以闻，伏取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1233542_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年</a>　上辞免札子。作品：《辞免敕令所修书成转官第三札子》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年12月11日</a>　十二月十一日，在湖州。乞以所修书成转官回授兄梦求。上乞回授札子。作品：《乞回授敕令所修书成转官与兄监岳札子》<div id='poem_1233544' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233544' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233544?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞回授敕令所修书成转官与兄监岳劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年12月11日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233544")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233544_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233544'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233544'>臣今月初二日准尚书省劄子，以臣辞免转官恩命，奉圣旨，依累降诏旨不允者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233544_comment'></div>庀官无尺寸之功，难胜误赏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233544_comment'></div>沥恳有再三之渎，宜就严诛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233544_comment'></div>过蒙宽宥之恩，终閟矜从之旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233544_comment'></div>愧益深而汗溢，感弥极而涕流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233544_comment'></div>伏念臣家世至寒，资材甚下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233544_comment'></div>被服父兄之训，偶玷儒科；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233544_comment'></div>遭遇圣神之知，寖污政路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233544_comment'></div>比投闲散，犹荷记怜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233544_comment'></div>称效云何，侥倖如此，粉身碎首，曷足报偿？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233544_comment'></div>履薄临深，每知恐惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233544_comment'></div>辄恃天地包容之量，复陈犬马冒昧之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233544_comment'></div>重念臣兄右迪功郎、监潭州南岳庙某，少习艺文，久困场屋，晚沾恩命，甫列选阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1233544_comment'></div>念暮年手足之情，岂忘牵爱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1233544_comment'></div>顾平日肺肝之恳，不敢及私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1233544_comment'></div>兹缘异恩，庶均同气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1233544_comment'></div>仰祈圣造，曲轸天慈，特许以臣今来所转一官回授与臣兄某循转施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1233544_comment'></div>将侈朝廷之宠光，用增门户之荣耀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1233544_comment'></div>屡渎宸听，万死奚逃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1233544_comment'></div>臣无任瞻天望圣祈恩俟罪跼蹐屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1233544_comment'></div>谨具劄子奏请以闻，伏取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1233544_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年12月</a>　上谢表。作品：《转官许回授与兄谢表》<div id='poem_1233495' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233495' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233495?labeling=true' target='_blank'>转官许回授与兄谢表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233495")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233495_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233495'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233495'>陟冈之念，仰彻于聪明；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233495_comment'></div>出綍之言，俯加于眷奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233495_comment'></div>乃回公渥，以遂私情<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233495_comment'></div>伏念臣一远天墀，十移月籥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233495_comment'></div>齿衰撄疾，分宜屏于丘园；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233495_comment'></div>器溢挻灾，诚恐填于沟壑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233495_comment'></div>空守不移之志，长怀未报之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233495_comment'></div>曾谓微劳，遽叨殊宠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233495_comment'></div>顾事为之弥称，控避恳而莫谐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233495_comment'></div>爰念急难，冒陈迫切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233495_comment'></div>雨露之泽既沾被于同根，云汉之章复表扬于异数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233495_comment'></div>兄弟感泣，父老叹咨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233495_comment'></div>夫何差池，有此侥倖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1233495_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇皇帝陛下尧舜孝弟，文武忧勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1233495_comment'></div>赏以懋功，图日新于庶治；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1233495_comment'></div>化惟美俗，用风劝于多方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1233495_comment'></div>是致愿私，果蒙褒允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1233495_comment'></div>臣敢不体认德意，佩服训词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1233495_comment'></div>白首相依，喜益敦手足之爱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1233495_comment'></div>丹心犹在，誓将期顶踵之捐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1233495_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1233495_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年12月</a>　上谢宰执启。作品：《转官许回授于兄谢宰执启》<div id='poem_1233647' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233647' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233647?labeling=true' target='_blank'>转官许回授与兄谢宰执启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233647")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233647_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233647'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233647'>庀职无功，叨被公朝之宠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233647_comment'></div>抗章有请，愿为私室之营。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233647_comment'></div>仰承出綍之恩，俯慰陟冈之念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233647_comment'></div>兄弟感泣，父老叹咨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233647_comment'></div>伏念某起家寒微，涉世迂阔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233647_comment'></div>进踰涯分，自贻满溢之虞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233647_comment'></div>退省愆违，犹负颠隮之惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233647_comment'></div>至若成书之奏御，固已乞身而去朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233647_comment'></div>敢谓第名，例蒙朌赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233647_comment'></div>念事为之靡称，控恳避而莫谐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233647_comment'></div>爰念急难，冒陈迫切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233647_comment'></div>雨露之泽既沾被于同根，云汉之章复表扬于异数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233647_comment'></div>夫何侥倖，有此遭逢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1233647_comment'></div>兹盖伏遇某官直道事君，诚心好善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1233647_comment'></div>性惇孝友，用风劝于多方；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1233647_comment'></div>身任安危，将日新于庶治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1233647_comment'></div>过蒙矜恻，乃获褒俞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1233647_comment'></div>方收迹于山樊，第归恩于陶冶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1233647_comment'></div>铭镂之至，敷叙曷周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1233647_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1233647_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年1月5日</a>　正月，居湖州。初五，改提举万寿观兼侍读。上辞免札子。作品：《辞免除在京宫观侍读第一札子》<div id='poem_1233545' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233545' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233545?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免除在京宫观侍读第一劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1137年1月5日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233545")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233545_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233545'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233545'>臣今月□□日，准行在入内内侍省金字牌递到尚书省劄子，奉圣旨除臣提举万寿观兼侍读，日下起发赴行在所供职者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233545_comment'></div>闻命跼蹐，感涕交流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233545_comment'></div>伏念臣顷以锄耰固陋之质，误被眷知，擢自小官，至陪大政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233545_comment'></div>一毫无补，百谪有馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233545_comment'></div>仰蒙从欲之仁，俯徇投闲之请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233545_comment'></div>思愆里舍，仅阅岁时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233545_comment'></div>虽存阙之心，不忘造次；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233545_comment'></div>而归田之幸，甫迫衰残。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233545_comment'></div>敢图圣恩，骤加收召。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233545_comment'></div>露门劝读，殊庭奉祠，此在累朝实为贵老优贤之地，如臣碌碌，并冒宠除，分非所安，兢惶失措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233545_comment'></div>然方陛下亲乘戎辂，力图恢复之日，在臣子之义，岂不欲一望清光，少伸志愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233545_comment'></div>而叨尘非据，定致烦言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233545_comment'></div>深自省循，进退维谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1233545_comment'></div>伏望陛下特轸天慈，追寝成命，俾臣仍旧外祠，休养疾病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1233545_comment'></div>他日傥或未填沟壑，誓期糜殒，少答鸿私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1233545_comment'></div>臣近为感冒风湿，左足筋挛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1233545_comment'></div>日下起发未得，见服药调治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1233545_comment'></div>稍可支梧，即迤逦前路，听候指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1233545_comment'></div>谨具劄子陈免以闻，伏取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1233545_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年1月11日</a>　正月十一日，在湖州。下诏不允。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年1月12日</a>　正月十二日，在湖州。诏疾赴平江。<br /></div>

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年</a>　上到任谢表。作品：《谢知镇江府到任表》<div id='poem_1233482' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233482' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233482?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢知镇江府到任表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233482")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233482_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233482'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233482'>奉祠真馆，本避宠而投閒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233482_comment'></div>试守名邦，忽叨恩而任剧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233482_comment'></div>已布哀矜之诏，庶销愁恨之声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233482_comment'></div>下听民言，皆知上德<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233482_comment'></div>伏念臣衰羸多病，朴拙少文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233482_comment'></div>奋身无半面之交，最为孤立；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233482_comment'></div>遇主有一言之合，亟被深知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233482_comment'></div>向尘耳目之司，即受腹心之托。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233482_comment'></div>虽触犯忌讳，每恃包容；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233482_comment'></div>然排击奸邪，多招仇怨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233482_comment'></div>而臣忠在许国，义难徇人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233482_comment'></div>迨升铨总之曹，冞积颠隮之惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233482_comment'></div>稍求散地，俄奉俞音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1233482_comment'></div>一自去于朝班，已再更于年所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1233482_comment'></div>形潜穷谷，方追麋鹿之游；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1233482_comment'></div>梦入修门，空想鹓鸾之侣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1233482_comment'></div>敢图简记，复玷使令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1233482_comment'></div>矧此凋残之馀，居然控扼之要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1233482_comment'></div>江山犹昔，虽云襟带之存；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1233482_comment'></div>城郭已非，但见丘墟之积。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1233482_comment'></div>志徒策励，才岂堪任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1233482_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下器使群才，陶成庶类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1233482_comment'></div>念臣进繇新擢，姑务保全于始终；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1233482_comment'></div>察臣退在自安，更令扬历于中外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1233482_comment'></div>肉骨之恩逾厚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1233482_comment'></div>糜躯之报益坚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1233482_comment'></div>诚恐技穷，敢辞责重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1233482_comment'></div>谨当奉承德意，劳还缘亩之民；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1233482_comment'></div>凭藉威灵，和辑捍边之士，粗能办职，犹觊乞身。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1233482_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年</a>　上谢宰执启。作品：《知镇江府到任谢宰执启》<div id='poem_1233634' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233634' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233634?labeling=true' target='_blank'>知镇江府到任谢宰执启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233634")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233634_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233634'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233634'>起之閒馆，付以名城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233634_comment'></div>井邑丘墟，未变创残之俗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233634_comment'></div>江山襟带，犹为形胜之区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233634_comment'></div>宿师方折于遐冲，谋帅乃推于庸品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233634_comment'></div>才虽靡称，恩则有归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233634_comment'></div>此盖伏遇某官柱石邦图，蓍龟国论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233634_comment'></div>以一夫不获为重任，以四方未靖为深忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233634_comment'></div>雅量镇浮，屹立中朝之望；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233634_comment'></div>元功定难，力摧外敌之锋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233634_comment'></div>盖将扶大厦之颠，故尽掩群材之短。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233634_comment'></div>遂令驽钝，亦累埏镕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233634_comment'></div>既奔命以之官，庶收功而塞责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233634_comment'></div>然某衰羸多病，褊急少思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1233634_comment'></div>方当调发之烦，未免催科之拙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1233634_comment'></div>愿宽衔勒，觊脱简书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1233634_comment'></div>不失朝廷劳来之方，是为门阑收录之报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1233634_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1233634_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年</a>　有谢状。作品：《知镇江通用谢状》<div id='poem_1233631' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233631' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233631?labeling=true' target='_blank'>知镇江通用谢状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233631")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233631_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233631'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233631'>比者忽膺明命，宠付便藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233631_comment'></div>收迹山林之间，方图屏伏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233631_comment'></div>从事干戈之际，岂克堪任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233631_comment'></div>揣分知难，冒荣为惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233631_comment'></div>此盖某官推心忠厚，迪行端良。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233631_comment'></div>借馀论以嘘枯，致误恩之起废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233631_comment'></div>更蒙珍翰，用贲孤踪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233631_comment'></div>感愧之私，敷陈罔既。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233631_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1233631_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年</a>　在镇江，有回人贺启。作品：《知镇江回人贺启》<div id='poem_1233633' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233633' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233633?labeling=true' target='_blank'>知镇江回人贺启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233633")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233633_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233633'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233633'>比者忽膺明命，宠付便藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233633_comment'></div>收迹林泉之间，方图屏伏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233633_comment'></div>从事干戈之际，岂克堪任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233633_comment'></div>揣分知难，冒荣为惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233633_comment'></div>此盖某官壮猷排难，雅量包荒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233633_comment'></div>借馀论以嘘枯，致误恩之起废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233633_comment'></div>江山如故，方从仁里之游；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233633_comment'></div>雉堞相望，更托善邻之庇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233633_comment'></div>特贻珍翰，益贲孤踪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233633_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1233633_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年</a>　在镇江，有与人状。作品：《知镇江与户部姚侍郎先状》《知镇江与韩帅先状》<div id='poem_1233630' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233630' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_1233630'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233630'>比者误膺明命，宠付便藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233630_comment'></div>顾衰病之无庸，岂堪烦剧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233630_comment'></div>赖知怜之有素，遂托庇存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233630_comment'></div>即获参承，倍增欣抃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233630_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1233630_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1233632' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233632' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233632?labeling=true' target='_blank'>知镇江与韩帅先状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233632'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233632'>比者误膺明命，宠付便藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233632_comment'></div>久伏山林之间，岂堪烦剧；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233632_comment'></div>仰托节旄之下，庶获庇存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233632_comment'></div>属鞬将谒于辕门，削牍敢尘于记室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233632_comment'></div>依归之素，敷叙曷殚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233632_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1233632_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年3月</a>　三月，在镇江，作贺启。作品：《贺赵参政启》<div id='poem_1233629' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233629' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233629?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺赵参政启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233629")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233629_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233629'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233629'>伏审进登旧弼，参总繁机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233629_comment'></div>命下九天，驩腾万宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233629_comment'></div>窃惟自古祸乱之国，必生希世豪杰之才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233629_comment'></div>因时作兴，与民休息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233629_comment'></div>临巨川而未济，方俟舟航；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233629_comment'></div>扶大厦之将倾，必资柱石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233629_comment'></div>副上此意，非公而谁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233629_comment'></div>伏惟某官诚格天渊，忠存庙社。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233629_comment'></div>方严足以断大事，静重足以经远猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233629_comment'></div>直道而行，独立不惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233629_comment'></div>蹇蹇王臣之节，更变故而弥坚；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233629_comment'></div>赫赫师尹之瞻，遭谗邪而益著。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233629_comment'></div>挤之剧地，凛然威名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1233629_comment'></div>是致未央兴夜半之思，长安指日边之路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1233629_comment'></div>迨膺出綍，不俟解鞍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1233629_comment'></div>见管夷吾，谁复效楚囚之泣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1233629_comment'></div>用范武子，自然知晋盗之奔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1233629_comment'></div>争睹设施，预期戡定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1233629_comment'></div>岂特疲氓之引领，是为善类之倾心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1233629_comment'></div>矧此孤踪，尝叨异盼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1233629_comment'></div>方念一麾而去国，未能三贺以登门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1233629_comment'></div>抃跃私诚，倍万常品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1233629_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1233629_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年6月26日</a>　六月二十六日，在镇江。奏请镇江府贫户残欠苗米秋后拨还。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年</a>　知镇江府期间，召流民、使复业，恩威并行，治郡有方。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年7月2日</a>　七月初二，在镇江。以赵鼎荐，复除吏部尚书。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年7月</a>　上辞免状。作品：《辞免再除吏部尚书奏状》<div id='poem_1233513' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233513' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233513?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免再除吏部尚书奏状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233513")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233513_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233513'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233513'>右，臣今月初六日准尚书省劄子，奉圣旨除臣吏部尚书者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233513_comment'></div>闻命震惊，罔知所措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233513_comment'></div>伏念臣资材极陋，家世至寒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233513_comment'></div>亲逢圣明，躐寘通显。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233513_comment'></div>试之中外，顾五技之已穷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233513_comment'></div>考其初终，念一毫之何补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233513_comment'></div>省循涯分，孤负恩私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233513_comment'></div>理宜投劾以知非，否则丐閒而免咎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233513_comment'></div>缘臣到郡，方此阅时，恐涉避事之嫌，未敢抗章而请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233513_comment'></div>敢意冕旒之眷，尚矜簪履之遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233513_comment'></div>亟下诏除，俾司铨总。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233513_comment'></div>非臣糜殒，所克报偿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233513_comment'></div>便合引途，岂宜俟驾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1233513_comment'></div>而臣顷叨已试，自揣不能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1233513_comment'></div>虽寻绎弊端，稍加惩艾，然抵触仇偶，几致颠隮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1233513_comment'></div>今复冒居，重乖清议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1233513_comment'></div>况臣血气素弱，疾疢交攻，傥更贪于宠荣，将益挻于灾衅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1233513_comment'></div>不免俯披愚悃，仰彻聪闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1233513_comment'></div>冀轸天慈，收还恩命，除臣一在外宫观差遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1233513_comment'></div>庶公朝当授受之际，既曰得宜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1233513_comment'></div>而微臣处进退之间，亦为有据。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1233513_comment'></div>干冒天威，臣无任战灼屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1233513_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1233513_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年7月</a>　再上辞免状。作品：《辞免吏部第二状》<div id='poem_1233514' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233514' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233514?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免吏部第二状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233514")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233514_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233514'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233514'>右，臣今月十五日准进奏院递到诏书一道，已除臣吏部尚书，乘递马发来，赴行在供职者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233514_comment'></div>恭读训词，感涕交溢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233514_comment'></div>伏念臣草芥微贱，无他技能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233514_comment'></div>仰蒙陛下怜臣孤直，拔于稠人之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233514_comment'></div>遍尘华要，并冒宠荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233514_comment'></div>臣徒有拳拳欲报之心，而才分所局，虽勤何补？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233514_comment'></div>今者治郡累月，未有善状，孤负使令，愈怀震惕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233514_comment'></div>岂谓天慈曲加记录，召以一节，俾归旧班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233514_comment'></div>洪惟生死肉骨之恩，虽殒百身，曷能称塞？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233514_comment'></div>而臣已试无功，加之疾疢，尝具奏陈，乞追寝成命，改授臣一在外宫观差遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233514_comment'></div>伏望陛下廓天地之量，回日月之明，特降睿旨，检会臣前奏施行，庶安愚分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233514_comment'></div>臣只候向宗厚到本州交割职事，迤逦前路，听候指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233514_comment'></div>渎犯天威，臣无任惶惧战灼之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1233514_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1233514_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年7月21日</a>　七月二十一日，在镇江，以吏部尚书兼侍读。<br /></div>
-----end

href='/Writing/1233433?labeling=true' target='_blank'>招从伪士大夫诏<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴四年十二月十二日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1134年12月12日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_title_1233433_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233433'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233433'>朕惟靖康兵革之难，神器几坠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233433_comment'></div>天命有在，属于眇躬，夙夜兢兢，罔敢自逸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233433_comment'></div>期与尔士大夫共雪大耻，还我两宫，保有黎元，永庇中土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233433_comment'></div>而强敌侵轶，迫朕一隅，叛臣乘时，盗据京邑，使我缙绅，沦陷涂炭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233433_comment'></div>繇朕不德，以至于斯，北望伤心，收涕无所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233433_comment'></div>亦惟尔士大夫蒙祖宗休泽，服在周行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233433_comment'></div>其有失身伪廷，事非其主，顾驱胁使然，有不得已者，朕甚痛之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233433_comment'></div>故若张孝纯、李邺、李俦等内外亲族不废禄仕，每饬有司常加存恤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233433_comment'></div>朕之于尔厚矣，尔尚忍忘之耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233433_comment'></div>其能洗心易虑，束身以归，当复其爵秩，待遇如初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233433_comment'></div>或为奇谋秘画，立功自效，乃朌异赏，不限彝章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233433_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233433_comment'></div>逆顺之理，祸福之机，昭然甚明，要知所择。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1233433_comment'></div>朕方布大信以示天下，言不尔欺，有如皦日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1233433_comment'></div>咸务自省，体朕至怀。</div><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年1月3日</a>　正月初三，在平江，陈将帅和、能克敌之道。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年1月7日</a>　正月初七，在平江。陈历代皆有君子与小人，其要在处之得宜。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年1月17日</a>　正月十七日，在平江，草诏书。作品：《赐刘光世韩世忠张俊诏》<div id='poem_1233439' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233439' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233439?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐刘光世韩世忠张浚诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年1月17日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233439")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233439_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233439'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233439'>朕自渡江以来，志在恢复，深惟足食足兵之计，夙夜疚怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233439_comment'></div>凡财赋所入，未尝一毫妄费，悉用养兵而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233439_comment'></div>故比年训练，士卒精强，而器械亦皆犀利，比之曩昔，实不相侔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233439_comment'></div>是以去冬敌人之来，卒赖卿等极力捍御，致彼遁归，盖前此所未有也，朕甚嘉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233439_comment'></div>然中原之未复，二圣未还，而僭伪之徒，方挟强国之援，狡谋日急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233439_comment'></div>顾我所以胜之者，惟是上下内外合为一家，如报私仇，乃克有济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233439_comment'></div>傥或各以其职，自分彼此，日复一日，成功实难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233439_comment'></div>卿为国重臣，安危所系，谅必察此，不待朕言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233439_comment'></div>今国用空殚，民力耗竭，虽有司锱铢积累，而费出之数，日以寖广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233439_comment'></div>苟无以继，何以聚人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233439_comment'></div>每一念之，心常怵惕，想卿亦为朕虑及于此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233439_comment'></div>至于差辟官属，保明功赏，军须用度之类，更在精覈，勿至泛滥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233439_comment'></div>使赏当而爵禄不私，用足而资给不匮，则存养事力，渐图进取，朕与卿等同享无穷之利，顾不美哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1233439_comment'></div>布朕此意，卿宜悉之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1233439_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年1月28日</a>　正月二十八日，在平江。论英宗、渊圣皇帝御赐帅臣酒器故事。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='751d787b59e24e72b642efe88f6d8a2b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("751d787b59e24e72b642efe88f6d8a2b");'><span id='751d787b59e24e72b642efe88f6d8a2b_link' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233547?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为病未及朝见奏知劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1137年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233547")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233547_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233547'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233547'>臣近蒙圣恩，除臣提举万寿观兼侍读。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233547_comment'></div>臣以疾病馀生，愚陋朴拙，自度无以称塞眷知，夙夜惶惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233547_comment'></div>尝沥恳诚，乞寝成命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233547_comment'></div>而九日之间两奉诏书，四次被受御前金字牌降到圣旨指挥催促起发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233547_comment'></div>念方陛下戎辂亲巡之际，在臣子之义，迫于严命，不遑安处，遂力疾迤逦前来，已次行阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233547_comment'></div>然臣所患左足筋挛之疾，痛楚呻吟，至不可忍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233547_comment'></div>沿路服药调理，尚未全安，有妨久立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233547_comment'></div>欲于门外将息一两日，趁赴朝见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233547_comment'></div>臣无任战灼之至，谨具劄子奏闻，伏取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1233547_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年1月21日</a>　正月二十一日，除同知枢密院事。上辞免表。作品：《辞免同知枢密院事表》<div id='poem_1233496' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233496' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233496?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免除同知枢密院事表</a><span class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233496'>宠命骤加，方怀震惕；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233496_comment'></div>愚诚冒贡，未赐矜从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233496_comment'></div>敢忘犯上之诛，更罄由衷之恳<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233496_comment'></div>伏念臣顷以弱质，叨污近联。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233496_comment'></div>惊岁序之荐更，寖妨贤路；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233496_comment'></div>悼事功之蔑著，上负圣知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233496_comment'></div>所宜养疾于丘园，遂请辞荣于廊庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233496_comment'></div>仰繄全度，俯佚残骸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233496_comment'></div>岂图仄席之求，未忍遗簪之弃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233496_comment'></div>召趋宣室之对，擢奉露门之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233496_comment'></div>一望清光，再蒙殊用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233496_comment'></div>念进读清閒之职，犹惧滥居；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233496_comment'></div>顾本兵枢要之司，讵容虚受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1233496_comment'></div>上既关于国体，下必致于人言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1233496_comment'></div>伏望皇帝陛下曲轸天慈，特回渊听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1233496_comment'></div>察臣空疏已试之技，固自无庸；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1233496_comment'></div>怜臣尪残既老之身，岂能有补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1233496_comment'></div>追还成命，别选异才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1233496_comment'></div>倘忘反汗之嫌，必免旷官之悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1233496_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1233496_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年1月</a>　上辞免札子。作品：《辞免同知枢密院札子》<div id='poem_1233548' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233548' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233548?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免除同知枢密院劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1137年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233548")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233548_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233548'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233548'>臣准尚书省劄子，正月二十一日三省同奉圣旨，除臣同知枢密院事，仍降中使宣押赴院供职者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233548_comment'></div>闻命震惊，罔知所措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233548_comment'></div>窃以辅臣之任，国论所资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233548_comment'></div>况当用武之时，尤重本兵之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233548_comment'></div>欲赞能事，宜得伟人，庶协成谋，用戡多难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233548_comment'></div>如臣资材凡琐，性识瞀昏，智虑不足以度万事之宜，权略不足以应一时之变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233548_comment'></div>顷蒙圣奖，擢与政途。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233548_comment'></div>昧于谋国，已试无能，久冒殊荣，曾微薄效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233548_comment'></div>陛下略其碌碌尸位之罪，察其拳拳忧国之诚，得请外祠，甫踰旬月，遽颁召节，趣侍经帷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233548_comment'></div>既获望于威颜，即再申于愚悃，觊收踪迹，复返丘园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233548_comment'></div>岂图异除，荐及庸品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233548_comment'></div>承命之次，颤汗忧惶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233548_comment'></div>臣疾病交攻，衰残日迫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1233548_comment'></div>傥或更叨委任，必误眷知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1233548_comment'></div>伏望陛下特轸深慈，追还成命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1233548_comment'></div>畴咨人望，用厌舆情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1233548_comment'></div>庶资经济之谋，以成恢复之业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1233548_comment'></div>臣无任恳倒迫切之至，谨具劄子陈免以闻，伏取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1233548_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年1月</a>　上谢表。作品：《谢除同知枢密院事表》<div id='poem_1233498' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1233498' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1233498?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢除同知枢密院事表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1137年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(28554, "宋", "沈与求", "poem_title_1233498")'>沈与求</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1233498_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1233498'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1233498'>进陪帝学，方趋召节之严；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1233498_comment'></div>参秉国枢，俄被制纶之渥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1233498_comment'></div>牢辞弗获，冒处徒惭<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1233498_comment'></div>伏念臣顷以谫能，误膺殊眷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1233498_comment'></div>擢寘群贤之右，与闻庶政之几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1233498_comment'></div>过计拳拳，每欲谨后车之戒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1233498_comment'></div>空言落落，岂能济前箸之筹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1233498_comment'></div>更拘俎豆之闻，终昧甲兵之问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1233498_comment'></div>技乃止此，才则使然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1233498_comment'></div>恐孤负于明时，思退休于晚岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1233498_comment'></div>敢意宠私之未憖，亟从閒外而见收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1233498_comment'></div>遽传趣行，便朝赐对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1233498_comment'></div>授以本兵之任，赞夫经武之图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1233498_comment'></div>然臣已试何功，既老焉用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1233498_comment'></div>血诚甚渎，汗号莫回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1233498_comment'></div>虽驽马十驾之勤，非敢后也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1233498_comment'></div>而铅刀一割之利，其可再乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1233498_comment'></div>伛偻拜恩，趑趄就列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1233498_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下尧仁天大，汤德日新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1233498_comment'></div>延揽英雄，务兼收于群策；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1233498_comment'></div>恢复境土，期尽雪于大雠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1233498_comment'></div>遂致衰迟，亦叨图任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1233498_comment'></div>臣敢不益励诚节，旁咨智谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1233498_comment'></div>依日月之光，固难施于爝火；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1233498_comment'></div>感风云之会，将少效于秋毫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1233498_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1233498_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年2月12日</a>　二月十二日，在平江。赞高宗爱惜生灵。同日，篆谥宝。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
桐乡（崇德）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='b6cc02df306f40a5a103ecfdfc3007d5_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b6cc02df306f40a5a103ecfdfc3007d5");'><span id='b6cc02df306f40a5a103ecfdfc3007d5_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年</a>，49岁</div><div id='b6cc02df306f40a5a103ecfdfc3007d5' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年10月24日</a>　十月二十四日，高宗车驾发临安府，草诏书。同日，扈高宗至崇德县。论韩世忠连退金人，功劳甚大。<br /></div>
